\subsection{pos\_to\_colrow (\$0C25)}

Converts a packed map position (0--199) into separate column and row
values by dividing by~20.  The map is 20~columns wide, so
{\Tt{}column\ =\ pos\ mod\ 20\nwendquote} and {\Tt{}row\ =\ pos\ /\ 20\nwendquote}.

The loop repeatedly subtracts~20 (via {\Tt{}ADC\ {\textbackslash}{\#}{\textbackslash}{\$}EC\nwendquote} with carry clear,
since {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}EC\ =\ 256\ {\$}-{\$}\ 20\nwendquote}), counting iterations in~{\Tt{}Y\nwendquote}.  When the
subtraction underflows (carry clear on exit), it adds~20 back to recover
the remainder.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{225}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}}}\moddef{pos to colrow~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0C25
\nwlinkedidentc{POS_TO_COLROW}{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDY      #$00              ; row = 0
.loop:
    CLC
    ADC      #$EC              ; A -= 20 (unsigned)
    BCC      .done             ; underflow → remainder is negative
    INY                        ; row++
    BCS      .loop             ; always taken (carry set)
.done:
    ADC      #$14              ; add 20 back → A = column (remainder)
    RTS                        ; A = column (0-19), Y = row (0-9)
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{POS{\_}TO{\_}COLROW}}{POS:unTO:unCOLROW}{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{POS{\_}TO{\_}COLROW}}{POS:unTO:unCOLROW}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{226}\nwdocspar

\subsection{print\_mob\_name (\$0D8A)}

Loads the name pointer from bytes~0--1 of the mob record at~{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}F8/{\textbackslash}{\$}F9\nwendquote}
into~{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BC/{\textbackslash}{\$}BD\nwendquote}, then tail-calls the text centering routine
at~\$7705, which centers and prints the name on screen row~23.
Used by 13~callers throughout the combat and interaction code.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{227}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-U2DT53IODGLRLPVDYRFI4YX3IQ000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-U2DT53IODGLRLPVDYRFI4YX3IQ000000-1}}}\moddef{print mob name~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-U2DT53IODGLRLPVDYRFI4YX3IQ000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0D8A
\nwlinkedidentc{PRINT_MOB_NAME}{PYNWmai0-U2DT53IODGLRLPVDYRFI4YX3IQ000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDY     #$00                    ; \\
    LDA     ($F8),Y                 ;  | $BC/$BD = bytes 0-1 of ($F8)
    STA     $BC                     ;  | (name string pointer)
    INY                             ;  |
    LDA     ($F8),Y                 ;  |
    STA     $BD                     ; /
    JMP     $7705                   ; center and print on row 23
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{PRINT{\_}MOB{\_}NAME}}{PRINT:unMOB:unNAME}{PYNWmai0-U2DT53IODGLRLPVDYRFI4YX3IQ000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{PRINT{\_}MOB{\_}NAME}}{PRINT:unMOB:unNAME}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{228}\nwdocspar

\subsection{colrow\_to\_pos (\$0D98)}

The inverse of {\Tt{}POS{\textbackslash}{\_}TO{\textbackslash}{\_}COLROW\nwendquote}: converts a column in~A and row in~Y
to a linear map position {\Tt{}A\ =\ col\ +\ row\ *\ 20\nwendquote}.  The carry is cleared
once on entry; thereafter the loop adds~20 per row and exits early if
carry occurs (overflow past 255).

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{229}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-YXZOC7KQXOV5OPKZ6P7KWNTLUM000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-YXZOC7KQXOV5OPKZ6P7KWNTLUM000000-1}}}\moddef{colrow to pos~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-YXZOC7KQXOV5OPKZ6P7KWNTLUM000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0D98
\nwlinkedidentc{COLROW_TO_POS}{PYNWmai0-YXZOC7KQXOV5OPKZ6P7KWNTLUM000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    CLC
.loop:
    DEY                         ; row--
    BPL     .add                ; still >= 0 → add another 20
    RTS                         ; Y exhausted, A = result
.add:
    ADC     #$14                ; A += 20
    BCC     .loop               ; no overflow → continue
                                ; carry set → return (overflow)
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{COLROW{\_}TO{\_}POS}}{COLROW:unTO:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-YXZOC7KQXOV5OPKZ6P7KWNTLUM000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{COLROW{\_}TO{\_}POS}}{COLROW:unTO:unPOS}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{230}\nwdocspar

\subsection{num\_to\_decimal (\$0DA1)}

Converts a 16-bit unsigned value in~{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BC/{\textbackslash}{\$}BD\nwendquote} to up to 5~ASCII
decimal digits, stored sequentially at {\Tt{}{\$}({\textbackslash}{\$}BA),Y{\$}\nwendquote} (with Y incrementing).
Leading zeros are suppressed unless the value is exactly zero (prints
``0'').  The output uses Apple~II high-ASCII ($\$B0$--$\$B9$).

The driver at~\$0DA1 calls the digit-extraction helper at~\$0DE1 five
times with divisors 10000, 1000, 100, 10, and~1.  The helper performs
repeated subtraction of {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}5A1C/{\textbackslash}{\$}5A1D\nwendquote} from {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BC/{\textbackslash}{\$}BD\nwendquote}, counting
iterations as the digit value.

A second entry point at~{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}0DA4\nwendquote} (1~caller) skips the initialization
of~Y and the leading-zero flag, allowing the caller to control the
starting output position and suppression behavior.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{231}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-NDZSG4V5NI575YZRAEMOIOV6CM000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-NDZSG4V5NI575YZRAEMOIOV6CM000000-1}}}\moddef{num to decimal~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-NDZSG4V5NI575YZRAEMOIOV6CM000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0DA1
\nwlinkedidentc{NUM_TO_DECIMAL}{PYNWmai0-NDZSG4V5NI575YZRAEMOIOV6CM000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDY     #$00                    ; output index = 0
    STY     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_LEADING}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}             ; leading-zero flag = 0 (suppress)
\nwlinkedidentc{NUM_TO_DECIMAL_CONT}{PYNWmai0-NDZSG4V5NI575YZRAEMOIOV6CM000000-1}:
    LDA     #$10                    ; \\  divisor = $2710 = 10000
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_DIVISOR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}             ;  |
    LDA     #$27                    ;  |
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_DIVISOR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}+1           ; /
    JSR     .extract_digit          ; ten-thousands digit
    LDA     #$E8                    ; \\  divisor = $03E8 = 1000
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_DIVISOR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}             ;  |
    LDA     #$03                    ;  |
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_DIVISOR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}+1           ; /
    JSR     .extract_digit          ; thousands digit
    LDA     #$64                    ; \\  divisor = $0064 = 100
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_DIVISOR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}             ;  |
    LDA     #$00                    ;  |
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_DIVISOR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}+1           ; /
    JSR     .extract_digit          ; hundreds digit
    LDA     #$0A                    ; \\  divisor = $000A = 10
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_DIVISOR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}             ; /  (high byte already 0)
    JSR     .extract_digit          ; tens digit
    LDA     #$01                    ; \\  divisor = $0001 = 1
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_DIVISOR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}             ;  |
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_LEADING}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}             ; /  force output (no suppress)
    JSR     .extract_digit          ; ones digit
    RTS

; --- Digit extraction helper ($0DE1) ---
; Divides $BC/$BD by $5A1C/$5A1D via repeated subtraction.
; Stores ASCII digit at ($BA),Y. Suppresses leading zeros.
.extract_digit:
    LDA     #$B0                    ; digit = '0' (high ASCII)
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_DIGIT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}
.cmp_loop:
    LDX     #$01                    ; start comparing high byte
.cmp_x:
    LDA     $BC,X                   ; \\
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_DIVISOR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8},X           ;  | compare $BC/$BD with divisor
    BCC     .output                 ;  | if less, done (digit found)
    BNE     .subtract               ; /  if greater, subtract
    DEX                             ; \\  high bytes equal: check low
    BNE     .subtract               ; /  (if X was 1, now 0 -> recompare)
    JMP     .cmp_x                  ;    compare low byte (X=0)
.subtract:
    SEC                             ; \\
    LDA     $BC                     ;  | $BC/$BD -= divisor
    SBC     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_DIVISOR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}             ;  |
    STA     $BC                     ;  |
    LDA     $BD                     ;  |
    SBC     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_DIVISOR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}+1           ;  |
    STA     $BD                     ; /
    INC     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_DIGIT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}               ; digit++
    JMP     .cmp_loop               ; try again (reset X=1)
.output:
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_DIGIT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}               ; \\
    CMP     #$B0                    ;  | if digit is '0'
    BNE     .store                  ;  |   and leading-zero suppress active
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_LEADING}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}             ;  |   skip output
    CMP     #$01                    ;  |
    BNE     .skip                   ; /
    LDA     #$B0                    ; (reload '0' for final digit)
.store:
    STA     ($BA),Y                 ; store digit at output buffer
    LDA     #$01                    ; \\  clear leading-zero suppress
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_LEADING}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}             ; /  (first nonzero digit seen)
.skip:
    INY                             ; advance output index
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{NUM{\_}TO{\_}DECIMAL}}{NUM:unTO:unDECIMAL}{PYNWmai0-NDZSG4V5NI575YZRAEMOIOV6CM000000-1}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{NUM{\_}TO{\_}DECIMAL{\_}CONT}}{NUM:unTO:unDECIMAL:unCONT}{PYNWmai0-NDZSG4V5NI575YZRAEMOIOV6CM000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{NUM{\_}TO{\_}DECIMAL}}{NUM:unTO:unDECIMAL}}\\{{\nwixident{NUM{\_}TO{\_}DECIMAL{\_}CONT}}{NUM:unTO:unDECIMAL:unCONT}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{NUM{\_}DIGIT}}{NUM:unDIGIT}}\\{{\nwixident{NUM{\_}DIVISOR}}{NUM:unDIVISOR}}\\{{\nwixident{NUM{\_}LEADING}}{NUM:unLEADING}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{NUM{\_}DIGIT}}{NUM:unDIGIT}{PYNWmai0-NDZSG4V5NI575YZRAEMOIOV6CM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{NUM{\_}DIVISOR}}{NUM:unDIVISOR}{PYNWmai0-NDZSG4V5NI575YZRAEMOIOV6CM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{NUM{\_}LEADING}}{NUM:unLEADING}{PYNWmai0-NDZSG4V5NI575YZRAEMOIOV6CM000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{232}\nwdocspar

\subsection{check\_encounter (\$0E25)}

Checks whether a given character (by char index in~{\Tt{}A\nwendquote}) is co-located
with a mob from an opposing faction.  Calls {\Tt{}FIND{\textbackslash}{\_}ENTITY{\textbackslash}{\_}AT{\textbackslash}{\_}POS\nwendquote} to
resolve the character to a mob pointer, then walks the group chain via
{\Tt{}FIND{\textbackslash}{\_}MOB{\textbackslash}{\_}AT{\textbackslash}{\_}SAME{\textbackslash}{\_}POS\nwendquote} looking for another mob at the same map
position.  Candidate mobs must have byte~6 bits~5--0~$\ge3$ (active mob
type) and be from a different faction (checked via {\Tt{}CHECK{\textbackslash}{\_}HOSTILE\nwendquote}).

Result stored in {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}5A1F\nwendquote}:
\begin{itemize}
\item 0 --- no mob found at same position (or character is not a mob)
\item 1 --- found co-located mob but same faction (wrapped search)
\item 2 --- found co-located mob from opposing faction (enemy encounter)
\end{itemize}

Callers use the result to set or clear bit~2 of byte~\$0F of the
character's record, which appears to be a ``combat engaged'' flag.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{233}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-15}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{ENCOUNTER_RESULT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}        EQU     $5A1F   ; 0/1/2 from \nwlinkedidentc{CHECK_ENCOUNTER}{PYNWmai0-PIBYNYNPF7BMUKCGA5W4VJAN7E000000-1}
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{ENCOUNTER{\_}RESULT}}{ENCOUNTER:unRESULT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{ENCOUNTER{\_}RESULT}}{ENCOUNTER:unRESULT}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{CHECK{\_}ENCOUNTER}}{CHECK:unENCOUNTER}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CHECK{\_}ENCOUNTER}}{CHECK:unENCOUNTER}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{234}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{235}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-PIBYNYNPF7BMUKCGA5W4VJAN7E000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-PIBYNYNPF7BMUKCGA5W4VJAN7E000000-1}}}\moddef{check encounter~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-PIBYNYNPF7BMUKCGA5W4VJAN7E000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0E25
\nwlinkedidentc{CHECK_ENCOUNTER}{PYNWmai0-PIBYNYNPF7BMUKCGA5W4VJAN7E000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FIND_ENTITY_AT_POS}{PYNWmai0-PLJFN4SECKS5ALV334RXDZNCVU000000-1}      ; look up char → $BE/$BF
    LDA     $BF
    CMP     #$00
    BEQ     .none                   ; null pointer → return 0
    CMP     #$80
    BMI     .none                   ; not a mob (bit 7 clear) → return 0
    AND     #$7F                    ; clear mob flag
    STA     $F5                     ; \\ $F4/$F5 = mob data pointer
    LDA     $BE                     ;  |
    STA     $F4                     ; /
.search:
    LDA     $F4                     ; \\ $BC/$BD = current mob pointer
    STA     $BC                     ;  |
    LDA     $F5                     ;  |
    STA     $BD                     ; /
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FIND_MOB_AT_SAME_POS}{PYNWmai0-W6IHVD5ZPEGW5W37XACEDHSWVY000000-1}    ; find next mob at same position
    CMP     #$01
    BMI     .none                   ; 0 = no co-located mob → return 0
    BEQ     .friendly               ; 1 = found (wrapped) → return 1
    LDY     #$06                    ; result >= 2: found ahead
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ; byte 6 of found mob
    AND     #$3F                    ; bits 5-0
    CMP     #$03                    ; active mob type?
    BCC     .search                 ; no → skip, keep searching
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CHECK_HOSTILE}{PYNWmai0-GAQSOYZEBE3NQVLK37GI4L4NOY000000-1}           ; compare factions
    CMP     #$00
    BEQ     .search                 ; same faction → skip
    LDA     #$02                    ; enemy found → return 2
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{ENCOUNTER_RESULT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}
    RTS
.none:
    LDA     #$00
    BEQ     .store
.friendly:
    LDA     #$01
.store:
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{ENCOUNTER_RESULT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{CHECK{\_}ENCOUNTER}}{CHECK:unENCOUNTER}{PYNWmai0-PIBYNYNPF7BMUKCGA5W4VJAN7E000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{CHECK{\_}ENCOUNTER}}{CHECK:unENCOUNTER}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{CHECK{\_}HOSTILE}}{CHECK:unHOSTILE}}\\{{\nwixident{ENCOUNTER{\_}RESULT}}{ENCOUNTER:unRESULT}}\\{{\nwixident{FIND{\_}ENTITY{\_}AT{\_}POS}}{FIND:unENTITY:unAT:unPOS}}\\{{\nwixident{FIND{\_}MOB{\_}AT{\_}SAME{\_}POS}}{FIND:unMOB:unAT:unSAME:unPOS}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CHECK{\_}HOSTILE}}{CHECK:unHOSTILE}{PYNWmai0-PIBYNYNPF7BMUKCGA5W4VJAN7E000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ENCOUNTER{\_}RESULT}}{ENCOUNTER:unRESULT}{PYNWmai0-PIBYNYNPF7BMUKCGA5W4VJAN7E000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{FIND{\_}ENTITY{\_}AT{\_}POS}}{FIND:unENTITY:unAT:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-PIBYNYNPF7BMUKCGA5W4VJAN7E000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{FIND{\_}MOB{\_}AT{\_}SAME{\_}POS}}{FIND:unMOB:unAT:unSAME:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-PIBYNYNPF7BMUKCGA5W4VJAN7E000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{236}\nwdocspar

\subsection{find\_mob\_at\_same\_pos (\$0E6C)}

Walks the group chain starting from the current mob ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}F4/{\textbackslash}{\$}F5\nwendquote}),
looking for another mob at the same map position (byte~3 of mob data).
If the current mob is the last in the chain (byte~2 = 0), the search
wraps around to the first mob via the group head ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}FA/{\textbackslash}{\$}FB\nwendquote}).

Returns in~{\Tt{}A\nwendquote}:
\begin{itemize}
\item 0 --- no other mob at same position (full circle)
\item 1 --- found co-located mob (search wrapped past end of chain)
\item 2 --- found co-located mob ahead in the chain
\end{itemize}

On success, {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}F4/{\textbackslash}{\$}F5\nwendquote} is updated to point to the found mob.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{237}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-15}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-15}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-16}\nwenddeflinemarkup

\nwlinkedidentc{COLOCATE_LINK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-15}           EQU     $5A20   ; saved next-link (stop condition)
\nwlinkedidentc{COLOCATE_WRAPPED}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-15}        EQU     $5A22   ; 1 if wrapped, 2 if ahead

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{239}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-W6IHVD5ZPEGW5W37XACEDHSWVY000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-W6IHVD5ZPEGW5W37XACEDHSWVY000000-1}}}\moddef{find mob at same pos~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-W6IHVD5ZPEGW5W37XACEDHSWVY000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0E6C
\nwlinkedidentc{FIND_MOB_AT_SAME_POS}{PYNWmai0-W6IHVD5ZPEGW5W37XACEDHSWVY000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDY     #$03
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ; byte 3 = position of current mob
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{COLOCATE_POS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-15}
    DEY
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ; byte 2 = next link of current mob
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{COLOCATE_LINK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-15}
    STY     \nwlinkedidentc{COLOCATE_WRAPPED}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-15}        ; $5A22 = 2 (found ahead)
.check_link:
    CMP     #$00
    BNE     .resolve                ; has next → follow it
    LDY     #$01
    STY     \nwlinkedidentc{COLOCATE_WRAPPED}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-15}        ; wrapped to start
    INY                             ; Y = 2
    LDA     ($FA),Y                 ; byte 2 of group head = first mob
.resolve:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{GET_MOB_DATA}{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}            ; A = mob index → $BA/$BB
    LDY     #$02
    LDA     ($BA),Y                 ; byte 2 of resolved mob
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{COLOCATE_LINK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-15}           ; same next-link as original?
    BNE     .not_self
    LDA     #$00                    ; full circle → not found
    RTS
.not_self:
    INY                             ; Y = 3
    LDA     ($BA),Y                 ; byte 3 = position
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{COLOCATE_POS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-15}            ; same position as original?
    BEQ     .found
    DEY                             ; Y = 2
    LDA     ($BA),Y                 ; follow next link
    JMP     .check_link
.found:
    LDA     $BA                     ; \\ update $F4/$F5 to found mob
    STA     $F4                     ;  |
    LDA     $BB                     ;  |
    STA     $F5                     ; /
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{COLOCATE_WRAPPED}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-15}        ; return 1 (wrapped) or 2 (ahead)
    RTS

\subsection{check\_hostile (\$0EB1)}

Determines whether two mobs are hostile to each other by comparing their
faction classifications.  Reads byte~4 (appearance index) from the mob
at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}F4/{\textbackslash}{\$}F5\nwendquote} and the mob at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BC/{\textbackslash}{\$}BD\nwendquote}, converts each via
{\Tt{}APPEARANCE{\textbackslash}{\_}TO{\textbackslash}{\_}FONTCHAR\nwendquote} to get the font group (quotient of dividing
by~21), then classifies via {\Tt{}GET{\textbackslash}{\_}HOSTILITY\nwendquote}: groups 0--2 and~7 are
``friendly'' (Y=0), groups 3--6 are ``hostile'' (Y=1).

Returns {\Tt{}A\nwendquote}=1 if the two mobs are on different sides, {\Tt{}A\nwendquote}=0 if same.
When both are hostile (Y=1), they are still hostile to each other if
their font-char remainders differ (different hostile sub-factions).

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{241}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-16}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-16}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-15}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}\nwenddeflinemarkup

\nwlinkedidentc{HOSTILE_A}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-16}               EQU     $5A24   ; saved A from first \nwlinkedidentc{GET_HOSTILITY}{PYNWmai0-K464VGCUY2CZLM74XVNPX3KPKM000000-1}
\nwlinkedidentc{HOSTILE_Y}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-16}               EQU     $5A25   ; saved Y from first \nwlinkedidentc{GET_HOSTILITY}{PYNWmai0-K464VGCUY2CZLM74XVNPX3KPKM000000-1}

    ORG     $0EB1
\nwlinkedidentc{CHECK_HOSTILE}{PYNWmai0-GAQSOYZEBE3NQVLK37GI4L4NOY000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDY     #$04
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ; byte 4 of found mob (appearance)
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{HOSTILE_APP}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-16}
    LDA     ($BC),Y                 ; byte 4 of original mob (appearance)
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{APPEARANCE_TO_FONTCHAR}{PYNWmai0-ZV3SLJLMHDXQXGXKZHHC4ROVNQ000000-1}  ; → A=remainder, Y=group
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{GET_HOSTILITY}{PYNWmai0-K464VGCUY2CZLM74XVNPX3KPKM000000-1}           ; → Y=0 (friendly) or 1 (hostile)
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{HOSTILE_A}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-16}
    STY     \nwlinkedidentc{HOSTILE_Y}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-16}
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{HOSTILE_APP}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-16}             ; appearance of found mob
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{APPEARANCE_TO_FONTCHAR}{PYNWmai0-ZV3SLJLMHDXQXGXKZHHC4ROVNQ000000-1}

    CPY     #$00
    BEQ     .same                   ; both friendly → same side

    BNE     .different              ; different → hostile to each other
.same:
    LDA     #$00
    RTS
.different:
    LDA     #$01
    RTS

\subsection{get\_hostility (\$0EE3)}

Classifies a font group number (in~{\Tt{}Y\nwendquote}, from {\Tt{}APPEARANCE{\textbackslash}{\_}TO{\textbackslash}{\_}FONTCHAR\nwendquote})
as friendly or hostile.  Groups 0--2 and~7 are friendly (Y$\leftarrow$0),
groups 3--6 are hostile (Y$\leftarrow$1).  The value in~{\Tt{}A\nwendquote} is preserved.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{245}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-K464VGCUY2CZLM74XVNPX3KPKM000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-K464VGCUY2CZLM74XVNPX3KPKM000000-1}}}\moddef{get hostility~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-K464VGCUY2CZLM74XVNPX3KPKM000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0EE3
\nwlinkedidentc{GET_HOSTILITY}{PYNWmai0-K464VGCUY2CZLM74XVNPX3KPKM000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    CPY     #$03                    ; factions 0-2 = friendly
    BCC     .friendly
    CPY     #$07                    ; faction 7 = friendly
    BEQ     .friendly
    LDY     #$01                    ; factions 3-6 = hostile
    RTS
.friendly:
    LDY     #$00
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{GET{\_}HOSTILITY}}{GET:unHOSTILITY}{PYNWmai0-K464VGCUY2CZLM74XVNPX3KPKM000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{GET{\_}HOSTILITY}}{GET:unHOSTILITY}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{246}\nwdocspar

\subsection{check\_adjacent\_threats (\$0EF1)}

Checks the four cardinal neighbors of a map position for hostile mobs
and accumulates their combined threat level.  Input: {\Tt{}A\nwendquote}~= position
(0--199), {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}F8/{\textbackslash}{\$}F9\nwendquote}~= character record pointer,
{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BC/{\textbackslash}{\$}BD\nwendquote}~= character's mob data pointer.

For each adjacent position (left, right, up, down), calls
{\Tt{}SUM{\textbackslash}{\_}HOSTILE{\textbackslash}{\_}AT{\textbackslash}{\_}POS\nwendquote} to find hostile mobs not already in combat and
sum their strength (byte~5 bits~4--0) into {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}5A26\nwendquote}.  After checking
all neighbors, compares the accumulated threat against the character's
defense value (byte~5 bits~4--1 of the {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}F8\nwendquote} record).

Returns {\Tt{}A\nwendquote}=1 if defense~$\ge$~threat (safe), {\Tt{}A\nwendquote}=0 if overwhelmed.
The threat total remains in {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}5A26\nwendquote} for callers that check it directly.

Boundary checks prevent wrapping: position~0 has no left neighbor,
position~199 no right, positions~0--19 no up, positions~180--199 no down.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{247}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-16}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-18}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{ADJACENT_THREAT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}         EQU     $5A26   ; accumulated adjacent threat level
\nwlinkedidentc{ADJACENT_POS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}            EQU     $5A27   ; saved position for adjacency check
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{ADJACENT{\_}POS}}{ADJACENT:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{ADJACENT{\_}THREAT}}{ADJACENT:unTHREAT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{ADJACENT{\_}POS}}{ADJACENT:unPOS}}\\{{\nwixident{ADJACENT{\_}THREAT}}{ADJACENT:unTHREAT}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{248}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{249}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-M2GJAYSU46D74HRO2UCFKPPZIQ000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-M2GJAYSU46D74HRO2UCFKPPZIQ000000-1}}}\moddef{check adjacent threats~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-M2GJAYSU46D74HRO2UCFKPPZIQ000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0EF1
\nwlinkedidentc{CHECK_ADJACENT_THREATS}{PYNWmai0-M2GJAYSU46D74HRO2UCFKPPZIQ000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{ADJACENT_POS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}            ; save target position
    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{ADJACENT_THREAT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}         ; clear threat accumulator
    LDA     $F8                     ; \\ $BC/$BD = character record pointer
    STA     $BC                     ;  |
    LDA     $F9                     ;  |
    STA     $BD                     ; /
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ADJACENT_POS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}            ; reload position
    BEQ     .skip_left              ; position 0 → no left neighbor
    SEC
    SBC     #$01                    ; position - 1
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SUM_HOSTILE_AT_POS}{PYNWmai0-EVL7KQK3LF5HDEEDTHSJTZIQAM000000-1}      ; check left
.skip_left:
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ADJACENT_POS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}
    CMP     #$C7                    ; position 199?
    BEQ     .skip_right             ; → no right neighbor
    CLC
    ADC     #$01                    ; position + 1
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SUM_HOSTILE_AT_POS}{PYNWmai0-EVL7KQK3LF5HDEEDTHSJTZIQAM000000-1}      ; check right
.skip_right:
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ADJACENT_POS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}
    BMI     .do_up                  ; >= 128 → always has up neighbor
    CMP     #$14                    ; < 20?
    BMI     .skip_up                ; → no up neighbor
.do_up:
    SEC
    SBC     #$14                    ; position - 20
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SUM_HOSTILE_AT_POS}{PYNWmai0-EVL7KQK3LF5HDEEDTHSJTZIQAM000000-1}      ; check up
.skip_up:
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ADJACENT_POS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}
    BPL     .do_down                ; < 128 → always has down neighbor
    CMP     #$B4                    ; >= 180?
    BPL     .skip_down              ; → no down neighbor
.do_down:
    CLC
    ADC     #$14                    ; position + 20
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SUM_HOSTILE_AT_POS}{PYNWmai0-EVL7KQK3LF5HDEEDTHSJTZIQAM000000-1}      ; check down
.skip_down:
    LDY     #$05
    LDA     ($F8),Y                 ; byte 5 of character record
    ROR                             ; \\ bits 4-1 → defense value
    AND     #$0F                    ; /
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{ADJACENT_THREAT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}         ; compare with threat total
    BPL     .safe                   ; defense >= threat → safe
    LDA     #$00
    RTS                             ; return 0 = overwhelmed
.safe:
    LDA     #$01
    RTS                             ; return 1 = safe
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{CHECK{\_}ADJACENT{\_}THREATS}}{CHECK:unADJACENT:unTHREATS}{PYNWmai0-M2GJAYSU46D74HRO2UCFKPPZIQ000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{CHECK{\_}ADJACENT{\_}THREATS}}{CHECK:unADJACENT:unTHREATS}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{ADJACENT{\_}POS}}{ADJACENT:unPOS}}\\{{\nwixident{ADJACENT{\_}THREAT}}{ADJACENT:unTHREAT}}\\{{\nwixident{SUM{\_}HOSTILE{\_}AT{\_}POS}}{SUM:unHOSTILE:unAT:unPOS}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ADJACENT{\_}POS}}{ADJACENT:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-M2GJAYSU46D74HRO2UCFKPPZIQ000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ADJACENT{\_}THREAT}}{ADJACENT:unTHREAT}{PYNWmai0-M2GJAYSU46D74HRO2UCFKPPZIQ000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SUM{\_}HOSTILE{\_}AT{\_}POS}}{SUM:unHOSTILE:unAT:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-M2GJAYSU46D74HRO2UCFKPPZIQ000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{250}\nwdocspar

\subsection{sum\_hostile\_at\_pos (\$0F49)}

Finds all hostile mobs at a given map position and adds their strength
to the threat accumulator {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}5A26\nwendquote}.  Input: {\Tt{}A\nwendquote}~= position,
{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BC/{\textbackslash}{\$}BD\nwendquote}~= reference mob for faction comparison.

For each mob found at the position, checks hostility via
{\Tt{}CHECK{\textbackslash}{\_}HOSTILE\nwendquote} and skips mobs that are already combat-engaged
(bit~2 of byte~\$0F set).  Hostile mobs contribute their strength
(byte~5 bits~4--0) to the running total, clamped at~127.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{251}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-EVL7KQK3LF5HDEEDTHSJTZIQAM000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-EVL7KQK3LF5HDEEDTHSJTZIQAM000000-1}}}\moddef{sum hostile at pos~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-EVL7KQK3LF5HDEEDTHSJTZIQAM000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0F49
\nwlinkedidentc{SUM_HOSTILE_AT_POS}{PYNWmai0-EVL7KQK3LF5HDEEDTHSJTZIQAM000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FIND_ENTITY_AT_POS}{PYNWmai0-PLJFN4SECKS5ALV334RXDZNCVU000000-1}      ; A = position → $BE/$BF
    LDA     $BF
    BEQ     .done                   ; null → nothing here
    CMP     #$80
    BMI     .done                   ; not a mob → skip
    AND     #$7F                    ; clear mob flag
    STA     $F5                     ; \\ $F4/$F5 = mob data pointer
    LDA     $BE                     ;  |
    STA     $F4                     ; /
.check_mob:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CHECK_HOSTILE}{PYNWmai0-GAQSOYZEBE3NQVLK37GI4L4NOY000000-1}           ; is this mob hostile to ($BC)?
    CMP     #$00
    BEQ     .next                   ; not hostile → skip
    LDY     #$0F
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ; byte $0F of mob
    AND     #$04                    ; bit 2 = combat engaged flag
    BNE     .next                   ; already in combat → skip
    LDY     #$05
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ; byte 5 of mob
    AND     #$1F                    ; bits 4-0 = strength
    CLC
    ADC     \nwlinkedidentc{ADJACENT_THREAT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}         ; accumulate threat
    BPL     .store
    LDA     #$7F                    ; clamp to 127
.store:
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{ADJACENT_THREAT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}
.next:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FIND_MOB_AT_SAME_POS}{PYNWmai0-W6IHVD5ZPEGW5W37XACEDHSWVY000000-1}    ; find next mob at same position
    CMP     #$02
    BEQ     .check_mob              ; more mobs → check them too
.done:
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SUM{\_}HOSTILE{\_}AT{\_}POS}}{SUM:unHOSTILE:unAT:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-EVL7KQK3LF5HDEEDTHSJTZIQAM000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SUM{\_}HOSTILE{\_}AT{\_}POS}}{SUM:unHOSTILE:unAT:unPOS}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{ADJACENT{\_}THREAT}}{ADJACENT:unTHREAT}}\\{{\nwixident{CHECK{\_}HOSTILE}}{CHECK:unHOSTILE}}\\{{\nwixident{FIND{\_}ENTITY{\_}AT{\_}POS}}{FIND:unENTITY:unAT:unPOS}}\\{{\nwixident{FIND{\_}MOB{\_}AT{\_}SAME{\_}POS}}{FIND:unMOB:unAT:unSAME:unPOS}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ADJACENT{\_}THREAT}}{ADJACENT:unTHREAT}{PYNWmai0-EVL7KQK3LF5HDEEDTHSJTZIQAM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CHECK{\_}HOSTILE}}{CHECK:unHOSTILE}{PYNWmai0-EVL7KQK3LF5HDEEDTHSJTZIQAM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{FIND{\_}ENTITY{\_}AT{\_}POS}}{FIND:unENTITY:unAT:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-EVL7KQK3LF5HDEEDTHSJTZIQAM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{FIND{\_}MOB{\_}AT{\_}SAME{\_}POS}}{FIND:unMOB:unAT:unSAME:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-EVL7KQK3LF5HDEEDTHSJTZIQAM000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{252}\nwdocspar

\subsection{compute\_scene\_ptr (\$0C32)}

Computes a pointer into the game data from a 1-based scene index in~A.
Each scene record is 16 bytes.  The result
{\Tt{}{\$}BA/{\$}BB\ =\ ({\$}4000)\ +\ (index\ -\ 1)\ {\textbackslash}times\ 16{\$}\nwendquote} is stored in {\Tt{}{\$}BA\nwendquote}/{\Tt{}{\$}BB\nwendquote},
where {\Tt{}{\$}4000/{\$}4001\nwendquote} holds the base address of the scene table.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{253}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-AW5VLYKLITE6VBTFNOR2WD6FNQ000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-AW5VLYKLITE6VBTFNOR2WD6FNQ000000-1}}}\moddef{compute scene ptr~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-AW5VLYKLITE6VBTFNOR2WD6FNQ000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0C32
\nwlinkedidentc{COMPUTE_SCENE_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AW5VLYKLITE6VBTFNOR2WD6FNQ000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    CLC
    ADC     #$FF                    ; A = index - 1
    ROL     A                       ; \\
    ROL     A                       ;  | rotate left 4 times
    ROL     A                       ;  | = multiply by 16 (with carry)
    ROL     A                       ; /
    TAY                             ; save intermediate
    ROL     A                       ; one more rotate
    AND     #$0F                    ; high nybble → page offset
    CLC
    ADC     $4001                   ; add base page
    STA     $BB                     ; high byte
    TYA
    AND     #$F0                    ; low nybble → byte offset
    CLC
    ADC     $4000                   ; add base offset
    STA     $BA                     ; low byte
    BCC     .done
    INC     $BB                     ; carry
.done:
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{COMPUTE{\_}SCENE{\_}PTR}}{COMPUTE:unSCENE:unPTR}{PYNWmai0-AW5VLYKLITE6VBTFNOR2WD6FNQ000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{COMPUTE{\_}SCENE{\_}PTR}}{COMPUTE:unSCENE:unPTR}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{254}\nwdocspar

\subsection{appearance\_to\_fontchar (\$0CF7)}

Converts a mob appearance index (byte~4 of mob data) into a font
character number.  The custom font has 120 characters in groups of~32,
but only 21~mob glyphs occupy each group (characters 1--21 and 33--36).
Characters 5--21 repeat cyclically for higher appearance values.

The routine divides the appearance value by~21 (via repeated subtraction
of~21), producing a quotient in~{\Tt{}Y\nwendquote} and a 1-based remainder in~{\Tt{}A\nwendquote}.
If the remainder is~$\ge5$, it is returned directly.  If~$<5$ and the
quotient is nonzero, 32 is added to index into the next font group.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{255}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ZV3SLJLMHDXQXGXKZHHC4ROVNQ000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ZV3SLJLMHDXQXGXKZHHC4ROVNQ000000-1}}}\moddef{appearance to fontchar~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ZV3SLJLMHDXQXGXKZHHC4ROVNQ000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0CF7
\nwlinkedidentc{APPEARANCE_TO_FONTCHAR}{PYNWmai0-ZV3SLJLMHDXQXGXKZHHC4ROVNQ000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDY      #$00              ; Y = quotient (font group)
.loop:
    CLC
    ADC      #$EB              ; A -= 21 (unsigned: $EB = 256-21)
    BCC      .done             ; underflow → done dividing
    INY                        ; group++
    BCS      .loop             ; always taken
.done:
    ADC      #$16              ; restore remainder+1 (carry clear, so +22)
    CMP      #$05              ; remainder >= 5?
    BCC      .low              ; no → check group
    RTS                        ; yes → return as-is (chars 5-21)
.low:
    CPY      #$00              ; first group?
    BEQ      .ret              ; yes → return as-is (chars 1-4)
    CLC
    ADC      #$20              ; add 32 → next font group (chars 33-36)
.ret:
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{APPEARANCE{\_}TO{\_}FONTCHAR}}{APPEARANCE:unTO:unFONTCHAR}{PYNWmai0-ZV3SLJLMHDXQXGXKZHHC4ROVNQ000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{APPEARANCE{\_}TO{\_}FONTCHAR}}{APPEARANCE:unTO:unFONTCHAR}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{256}\nwdocspar

\subsection{delay\_with\_animation (\$0D10)}

Delays for a configurable duration while keeping the status window
animation running.  Loads an iteration count from {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}7ABF\nwendquote} and calls
{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}0D30\nwendquote} (the per-tick animation/wait handler) that many times.
Each call to {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}0D30\nwendquote} ticks an animation counter, runs a timed wait
via the ROM {\Tt{}WAIT\nwendquote} routine, and advances the animation frame when
the counter expires.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{257}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-18}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-18}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-17}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}\nwenddeflinemarkup

\subsection{tick\_anim\_counter (\$0D1E)}

Decrements the animation frame counter at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}7AAF\nwendquote}.  When it reaches
zero, calls {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}74CB\nwendquote} to advance the animation frame.  Then reloads
the wait loop count from the timing table at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}7AB0\nwendquote} (indexed by
the current animation index at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}7ABD\nwendquote}) into {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}5A8C\nwendquote}.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{261}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-18}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-20}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{ANIM_FRAME_CTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}          EQU     $7AAF   ; animation frame countdown
\nwlinkedidentc{ANIM_INDEX}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}              EQU     $7ABD   ; current animation table index
\nwlinkedidentc{ANIM_WAIT_TABLE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}         EQU     $7AB0   ; per-frame wait counts (indexed)
\nwlinkedidentc{ANIM_FRAME_TABLE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}        EQU     $7AB6   ; per-frame frame counts (indexed)
\nwlinkedidentc{WAIT_LOOP_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}         EQU     $5A8C   ; inner wait loop counter
\nwlinkedidentc{WAIT_DURATION}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}           EQU     $7AAD   ; ROM WAIT duration parameter
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{ANIM{\_}FRAME{\_}CTR}}{ANIM:unFRAME:unCTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{ANIM{\_}FRAME{\_}TABLE}}{ANIM:unFRAME:unTABLE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{ANIM{\_}INDEX}}{ANIM:unINDEX}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{ANIM{\_}WAIT{\_}TABLE}}{ANIM:unWAIT:unTABLE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{WAIT{\_}DURATION}}{WAIT:unDURATION}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{WAIT{\_}LOOP{\_}COUNT}}{WAIT:unLOOP:unCOUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}\eatline

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{263}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-252H4ITL77INYHCEW5TFC3PMYE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-252H4ITL77INYHCEW5TFC3PMYE000000-1}}}\moddef{tick anim counter~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-252H4ITL77INYHCEW5TFC3PMYE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0D1E
\nwlinkedidentc{TICK_ANIM_COUNTER}{PYNWmai0-252H4ITL77INYHCEW5TFC3PMYE000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    DEC     \nwlinkedidentc{ANIM_FRAME_CTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}          ; tick frame counter
    BNE     .reload                 ; not zero → just reload wait count
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DRAW_BLINK_ALT}{PYNWmai0-D5AO3JLSN7XCTR2JDD26LFVLVU000000-1}          ; counter hit zero → draw alt char
.reload:

    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ANIM_WAIT_TABLE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19},X       ; look up wait count for this frame
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{WAIT_LOOP_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}         ; store for timed_wait to use
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{TICK{\_}ANIM{\_}COUNTER}}{TICK:unANIM:unCOUNTER}{PYNWmai0-252H4ITL77INYHCEW5TFC3PMYE000000-1}\eatline

\subsection{anim\_tick\_and\_wait (\$0D30)}

Combined animation tick and wait.  Calls {\Tt{}TICK{\textbackslash}{\_}ANIM{\textbackslash}{\_}COUNTER\nwendquote} to
decrement the frame counter and set up the wait count, then calls
{\Tt{}TIMED{\textbackslash}{\_}WAIT\nwendquote} to burn time.  If the frame counter has reached zero
(meaning the animation frame expired), calls {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}74DD\nwendquote} to update the
display and reloads the frame counter from the frame table at
{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}7AB6\nwendquote}.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{265}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ITIZTAY463ZOFFOFSBK22AG34I000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ITIZTAY463ZOFFOFSBK22AG34I000000-1}}}\moddef{anim tick and wait~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ITIZTAY463ZOFFOFSBK22AG34I000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0D30
\nwlinkedidentc{ANIM_TICK_AND_WAIT}{PYNWmai0-ITIZTAY463ZOFFOFSBK22AG34I000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{TICK_ANIM_COUNTER}{PYNWmai0-252H4ITL77INYHCEW5TFC3PMYE000000-1}       ; tick counter, reload wait count
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{TIMED_WAIT}{PYNWmai0-TTL3BS3ZNAOH4GH5O7EQQ2NYYQ000000-1}              ; burn time
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ANIM_FRAME_CTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}          ; did frame counter expire?
    BEQ     .advance                ; yes → advance animation
    RTS                             ; no → return

.advance:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DRAW_BLINK_NORMAL}{PYNWmai0-CUGO4OOCVBOXMS5VIR3B3MURQE000000-1}       ; redraw blink char in normal video
    LDX     \nwlinkedidentc{ANIM_INDEX}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}              ; reload animation index
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ANIM_FRAME_TABLE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19},X      ; look up frame duration
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{ANIM_FRAME_CTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}          ; reset frame counter
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{ANIM{\_}TICK{\_}AND{\_}WAIT}}{ANIM:unTICK:unAND:unWAIT}{PYNWmai0-ITIZTAY463ZOFFOFSBK22AG34I000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{ANIM{\_}TICK{\_}AND{\_}WAIT}}{ANIM:unTICK:unAND:unWAIT}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{ANIM{\_}FRAME{\_}CTR}}{ANIM:unFRAME:unCTR}}\\{{\nwixident{ANIM{\_}FRAME{\_}TABLE}}{ANIM:unFRAME:unTABLE}}\\{{\nwixident{ANIM{\_}INDEX}}{ANIM:unINDEX}}\\{{\nwixident{DRAW{\_}BLINK{\_}NORMAL}}{DRAW:unBLINK:unNORMAL}}\\{{\nwixident{TICK{\_}ANIM{\_}COUNTER}}{TICK:unANIM:unCOUNTER}}\\{{\nwixident{TIMED{\_}WAIT}}{TIMED:unWAIT}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ANIM{\_}FRAME{\_}CTR}}{ANIM:unFRAME:unCTR}{PYNWmai0-ITIZTAY463ZOFFOFSBK22AG34I000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ANIM{\_}FRAME{\_}TABLE}}{ANIM:unFRAME:unTABLE}{PYNWmai0-ITIZTAY463ZOFFOFSBK22AG34I000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ANIM{\_}INDEX}}{ANIM:unINDEX}{PYNWmai0-ITIZTAY463ZOFFOFSBK22AG34I000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{DRAW{\_}BLINK{\_}NORMAL}}{DRAW:unBLINK:unNORMAL}{PYNWmai0-ITIZTAY463ZOFFOFSBK22AG34I000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TICK{\_}ANIM{\_}COUNTER}}{TICK:unANIM:unCOUNTER}{PYNWmai0-ITIZTAY463ZOFFOFSBK22AG34I000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TIMED{\_}WAIT}}{TIMED:unWAIT}{PYNWmai0-ITIZTAY463ZOFFOFSBK22AG34I000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{266}\nwdocspar

\subsection{timed\_wait (\$0D49)}

Calls the ROM {\Tt{}WAIT\nwendquote} wrapper {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}0D58\nwendquote} repeatedly, decrementing
{\Tt{}WAIT{\textbackslash}{\_}LOOP{\textbackslash}{\_}COUNT\nwendquote} until it reaches zero.  If the count is already
zero on entry, returns immediately.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{267}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-TTL3BS3ZNAOH4GH5O7EQQ2NYYQ000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-TTL3BS3ZNAOH4GH5O7EQQ2NYYQ000000-1}}}\moddef{timed wait~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-TTL3BS3ZNAOH4GH5O7EQQ2NYYQ000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0D49
\nwlinkedidentc{TIMED_WAIT}{PYNWmai0-TTL3BS3ZNAOH4GH5O7EQQ2NYYQ000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{WAIT_LOOP_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}         ; anything to wait for?
    BNE     .wait                   ; yes → enter wait loop
    RTS                             ; no → return immediately

.wait:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CALL_ROM_WAIT}{PYNWmai0-NSI5UN2SREUW3YMCOFD6FHUKNQ000000-1}           ; delay one unit
    DEC     \nwlinkedidentc{WAIT_LOOP_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}         ; decrement counter
    BNE     .wait                   ; loop until zero
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{TIMED{\_}WAIT}}{TIMED:unWAIT}{PYNWmai0-TTL3BS3ZNAOH4GH5O7EQQ2NYYQ000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{TIMED{\_}WAIT}}{TIMED:unWAIT}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{CALL{\_}ROM{\_}WAIT}}{CALL:unROM:unWAIT}}\\{{\nwixident{WAIT{\_}LOOP{\_}COUNT}}{WAIT:unLOOP:unCOUNT}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CALL{\_}ROM{\_}WAIT}}{CALL:unROM:unWAIT}{PYNWmai0-TTL3BS3ZNAOH4GH5O7EQQ2NYYQ000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{WAIT{\_}LOOP{\_}COUNT}}{WAIT:unLOOP:unCOUNT}{PYNWmai0-TTL3BS3ZNAOH4GH5O7EQQ2NYYQ000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{268}\nwdocspar

\subsection{call\_rom\_wait (\$0D58)}

Loads the wait duration from {\Tt{}WAIT{\textbackslash}{\_}DURATION\nwendquote} and jumps to the
Apple~II ROM {\Tt{}WAIT\nwendquote} routine at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}FCA8\nwendquote}, which delays for
approximately $A \times 2.5 + 13.5$ microseconds.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{269}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-20}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-20}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-19}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{ROM_WAIT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-20}                EQU     $FCA8   ; Apple II ROM WAIT routine
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{ROM{\_}WAIT}}{ROM:unWAIT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-20}\eatline

\section{Text renderer}
\label{sec:text_renderer}

Reads a byte stream from the pointer at {\Tt{}{\$}06/{\$}07\nwendquote} and renders
characters on the hi-res screen.  It maintains column/row state and
supports several control codes.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{273}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-20}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{TEXT_RIGHT_MARGIN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}        EQU     $5A96   ; right margin column for text wrap
\nwlinkedidentc{TEXT_LEFT_MARGIN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}         EQU     $5A97   ; left margin column for text wrap
\nwlinkedidentc{TEXT_STREAM_IDX}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}          EQU     \nwlinkedidentc{TEXT_STREAM_IDX}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}   ; saved Y index into byte stream
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}LEFT{\_}MARGIN}}{TEXT:unLEFT:unMARGIN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}RIGHT{\_}MARGIN}}{TEXT:unRIGHT:unMARGIN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}STREAM{\_}IDX}}{TEXT:unSTREAM:unIDX}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}LEFT{\_}MARGIN}}{TEXT:unLEFT:unMARGIN}}\\{{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}RIGHT{\_}MARGIN}}{TEXT:unRIGHT:unMARGIN}}\\{{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}STREAM{\_}IDX}}{TEXT:unSTREAM:unIDX}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{274}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{275}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4PQFNHIY4HEZD756HZHHCIBVCA000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4PQFNHIY4HEZD756HZHHCIBVCA000000-1}}}\moddef{text renderer~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4PQFNHIY4HEZD756HZHHCIBVCA000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $6C8E
\nwlinkedidentc{TEXT_RENDERER}{PYNWmai0-4PQFNHIY4HEZD756HZHHCIBVCA000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDY     #$00
.init:
    LDA     #$02
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{TEXT_LEFT_MARGIN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}         ; left margin = 2
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{FONT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-3}                ; current column = 2
    LDA     #$12
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{TEXT_RIGHT_MARGIN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}       ; right margin = $12 (18)
    LDA     #$01
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{FONT_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-3}                ; current row = 1

    ; --- Main byte-reading loop ---
.fetch:
    LDA     ($06),Y                 ; read byte from stream
    BMI     .set_pos                ; bit 7 set → position command
    CMP     #$7F
    BNE     .not_end
    RTS                             ; $7F = end of stream

.not_end:
    CMP     #$7E
    BEQ     .pause                  ; $7E = pause
    CMP     #$7D
    BEQ     .reset                  ; $7D = reset to full-screen mode

    ; --- Character output ---
    STY     \nwlinkedidentc{TEXT_STREAM_IDX}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}                   ; save stream index
    STA     FONT_CHARNUM            ; character code
    LDA     #$02
    STA     FONT_CHARSET            ; character width = 2
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{PRINT_FONTCHAR}{PYNWmai0-QXEI7WLLMAMTCDDRNOTIC7PULU000000-1}          ; draw at current position
    INC     \nwlinkedidentc{FONT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-3}                ; advance column
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{FONT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-3}
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{TEXT_RIGHT_MARGIN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}       ; past right margin?
    BCC     .next                   ; no → continue
    INC     \nwlinkedidentc{FONT_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-3}                ; yes → next row
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{TEXT_LEFT_MARGIN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}        ;   reset column to left margin
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{FONT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-3}
.next:
    LDY     \nwlinkedidentc{TEXT_STREAM_IDX}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}                   ; restore stream index
    INY                             ; advance to next byte
    BNE     .fetch                  ; loop (max 256 per page)
    JMP     $1A31                   ; overflow handler

    ; --- Position command ($80-$FE) ---
.set_pos:
    AND     #$7F                    ; row = byte & $7F
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{FONT_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-3}
    INY
    LDA     ($06),Y                 ; next byte = column
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{FONT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-3}
    INY
    JMP     .fetch

    ; --- Pause ($7E): run script engine, show status bar ---
.pause:
    TYA                             ; \\
    PHA                             ;  | save stream index
    NOP
    LDX     #$06
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ENGINE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}           ; run attract script
    LDA     $06                     ; \\
    PHA                             ;  | save $06/$07 (stream pointer)
    LDA     $07                     ;  |
    PHA                             ; /
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_STATUS_BAR}{PYNWmai0-CAQTAAOHJTMFOSJ452F3J7I5JQ000000-1}      ; (clobbers $06/$07)
    PLA                             ; \\
    STA     $07                     ;  | restore $06/$07
    PLA                             ;  |
    STA     $06                     ; /
    PLA                             ; restore stream index
    TAY
    NOP
    INY                             ; advance past $7E
    JMP     .init                   ; reinit margins/position

    ; --- Reset ($7D): full-screen text mode ---
.reset:
    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{TEXT_LEFT_MARGIN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}         ; left margin = 0
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{FONT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-3}                ; column = 0
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{FONT_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-3}                ; row = 0
    LDA     #$14
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{TEXT_RIGHT_MARGIN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}       ; right margin = $14 (20)
    INY                             ; advance past $7D
    JMP     .fetch
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}RENDERER}}{TEXT:unRENDERER}{PYNWmai0-4PQFNHIY4HEZD756HZHHCIBVCA000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}RENDERER}}{TEXT:unRENDERER}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{DISPLAY{\_}STATUS{\_}BAR}}{DISPLAY:unSTATUS:unBAR}}\\{{\nwixident{FONT{\_}COL}}{FONT:unCOL}}\\{{\nwixident{FONT{\_}ROW}}{FONT:unROW}}\\{{\nwixident{PRINT{\_}FONTCHAR}}{PRINT:unFONTCHAR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}}\\{{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}LEFT{\_}MARGIN}}{TEXT:unLEFT:unMARGIN}}\\{{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}RIGHT{\_}MARGIN}}{TEXT:unRIGHT:unMARGIN}}\\{{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}STREAM{\_}IDX}}{TEXT:unSTREAM:unIDX}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{DISPLAY{\_}STATUS{\_}BAR}}{DISPLAY:unSTATUS:unBAR}{PYNWmai0-4PQFNHIY4HEZD756HZHHCIBVCA000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{FONT{\_}COL}}{FONT:unCOL}{PYNWmai0-4PQFNHIY4HEZD756HZHHCIBVCA000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{FONT{\_}ROW}}{FONT:unROW}{PYNWmai0-4PQFNHIY4HEZD756HZHHCIBVCA000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PRINT{\_}FONTCHAR}}{PRINT:unFONTCHAR}{PYNWmai0-4PQFNHIY4HEZD756HZHHCIBVCA000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}{PYNWmai0-4PQFNHIY4HEZD756HZHHCIBVCA000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}LEFT{\_}MARGIN}}{TEXT:unLEFT:unMARGIN}{PYNWmai0-4PQFNHIY4HEZD756HZHHCIBVCA000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}RIGHT{\_}MARGIN}}{TEXT:unRIGHT:unMARGIN}{PYNWmai0-4PQFNHIY4HEZD756HZHHCIBVCA000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}STREAM{\_}IDX}}{TEXT:unSTREAM:unIDX}{PYNWmai0-4PQFNHIY4HEZD756HZHHCIBVCA000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{276}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegindocs{277}\nwdocspar

\subsection{Control code summary}

\begin{center}
\begin{tabular}{cl}
\toprule
\thead{Byte} & \thead{Meaning} \\
\midrule
\$7D & Reset to full-screen mode (col=0, row=0, width=20) \\
\$7E & Pause: run script engine and status bar, then resume \\
\$7F & End of stream \\
\$80--\$FE & Set row (byte \& \$7F), next byte = column \\
Other & Character code for HRCG font \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
\end{center}

\subsection{Border data at \$7E2F}

The text renderer data at {\Tt{}STATUS{\textbackslash}{\_}BORDER{\textbackslash}{\_}DATA\nwendquote} draws a decorative
border for the status bar.  Characters \$33--\$41 are box-drawing glyphs
in the HRCG font.

\section{Resident bytecode interpreter (\$0500--\$07FF)}
\label{sec:resident_interp}

EALDR copies 768 bytes from {\Tt{}{\$}A300\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\$}A5FF\nwendquote} to {\Tt{}{\$}0500\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\$}07FF\nwendquote}
before entering the main program.  This region contains a second bytecode
interpreter, separate from the EALDR VM, that runs during gameplay and
the attract screen.  It uses the same XOR encryption scheme as the EALDR
VM (low byte XOR {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}03\nwendquote}, high byte XOR {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}D9\nwendquote}).

\subsection{attract\_loop (\$0569)}

The entry point for the resident interpreter.  Each iteration swaps
context (zero-page state) and dispatches one bytecode instruction.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{282}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}}}\moddef{attract loop~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0569
\nwlinkedidentc{ATTRACT_LOOP}{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CONTEXT_SWAP}{PYNWmai0-A5IY6LARV2ZVHGEJNTTVGGK3PU000000-1}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RESIDENT_DISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{ATTRACT_LOOP}{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}LOOP}}{ATTRACT:unLOOP}{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}LOOP}}{ATTRACT:unLOOP}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{CONTEXT{\_}SWAP}}{CONTEXT:unSWAP}}\\{{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CONTEXT{\_}SWAP}}{CONTEXT:unSWAP}{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{283}\nwdocspar

\subsection{context\_swap (\$06E0)}

Swaps 16 bytes between zero page {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}50\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}5F\nwendquote} and {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}07E5\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}07F4\nwendquote}.
This gives the resident interpreter its own private set of zero-page
temporaries that don't interfere with the main program.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{284}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-A5IY6LARV2ZVHGEJNTTVGGK3PU000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-A5IY6LARV2ZVHGEJNTTVGGK3PU000000-1}}}\moddef{context swap~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-A5IY6LARV2ZVHGEJNTTVGGK3PU000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $06E0
\nwlinkedidentc{CONTEXT_SWAP}{PYNWmai0-A5IY6LARV2ZVHGEJNTTVGGK3PU000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDX     #$0F
.loop:
    LDA     $50,X                   ; load ZP byte
    PHA                             ; save on stack
    LDA     $7E5,X                  ; load shadow byte
    STA     $50,X                   ; → ZP
    PLA                             ; recover old ZP byte
    STA     $7E5,X                  ; → shadow
    DEX
    BPL     .loop
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{CONTEXT{\_}SWAP}}{CONTEXT:unSWAP}{PYNWmai0-A5IY6LARV2ZVHGEJNTTVGGK3PU000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{CONTEXT{\_}SWAP}}{CONTEXT:unSWAP}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{285}\nwdocspar

\subsection{resident\_dispatch (\$06B3)}

Dispatches one bytecode instruction using a stack trick.  X and Y hold
the bytecode pointer from the previous iteration.  They are pushed onto
the stack at entry, then {\Tt{}PULL{\textbackslash}{\_}TWO{\textbackslash}{\_}RET{\textbackslash}{\_}ADDRS\nwendquote} rearranges the stack
so the saved X/Y values end up in {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}52/{\$}53\nwendquote} as the new bytecode pointer.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{286}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}}}\moddef{resident dispatch~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $06B3
\nwlinkedidentc{RESIDENT_DISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    TXA                             ; \\
    PHA                             ;  | save X, Y on stack
    TYA                             ;  | (these ARE the bytecode pointer)
    PHA                             ; /
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{PULL_TWO_RET_ADDRS}{PYNWmai0-ZQ3HACWSYBTTFFJTEM5GLS64PU000000-1}      ; rearrange stack, jump to .resume

    ; Control returns here via JMP ($54):
.resume:
    PLA                             ; \\  recover saved Y
    STA     $52                     ;  | $52/$53 = bytecode pointer
    PLA                             ;  | recover saved X
    STA     $53                     ; /

    LDY     #$04                    ; skip 4 bytes
.fetch:
    LDA     ($52),Y                 ; read opcode
    INY
    BNE     .no_carry
    INC     $53
.no_carry:
    TAX                             ; opcode → X (also saves position)
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{RESIDENT_DISPATCH_TABLE}{PYNWmai0-LZD7UO27WADGX7M4TS77RNCD74000000-1},X
    STA     resident_jmp+1          ; self-modify: JMP low byte
resident_jmp:
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{RESIDENT_DECODE_DISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-BGQWA2JRONNKYOAYDUITG47DXM000000-1} ; self-modified → $07xx
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{PULL{\_}TWO{\_}RET{\_}ADDRS}}{PULL:unTWO:unRET:unADDRS}}\\{{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DECODE{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDECODE:unDISPATCH}}\\{{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH{\_}TABLE}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH:unTABLE}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PULL{\_}TWO{\_}RET{\_}ADDRS}}{PULL:unTWO:unRET:unADDRS}{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DECODE{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDECODE:unDISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH{\_}TABLE}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH:unTABLE}{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{287}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegindocs{288}\nwdocspar

{\Tt{}PULL{\textbackslash}{\_}TWO{\textbackslash}{\_}RET{\textbackslash}{\_}ADDRS\nwendquote} pulls both return addresses from the stack
(its own and the caller's), increments each by 1 (since RTS pushes
addr\textminus{}1), and jumps through {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}54/{\$}55\nwendquote} back to the code
after the {\Tt{}JSR\nwendquote} in {\Tt{}RESIDENT{\textbackslash}{\_}DISPATCH\nwendquote}.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{289}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ZQ3HACWSYBTTFFJTEM5GLS64PU000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ZQ3HACWSYBTTFFJTEM5GLS64PU000000-1}}}\moddef{pull two ret addrs~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ZQ3HACWSYBTTFFJTEM5GLS64PU000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0738
\nwlinkedidentc{PULL_TWO_RET_ADDRS}{PYNWmai0-ZQ3HACWSYBTTFFJTEM5GLS64PU000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    PLA                             ; own return addr (low)
    STA     $54
    PLA                             ; own return addr (high)
    STA     $55
    PLA                             ; caller's return addr (low)
    STA     $52
    PLA                             ; caller's return addr (high)
    STA     $53
    INC     $52                     ; +1 (RTS pushed addr-1)
    INC     $54                     ; +1
    BNE     .done
    INC     $55                     ; carry
.done:
    JMP     ($54)                   ; jump back to .resume
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{PULL{\_}TWO{\_}RET{\_}ADDRS}}{PULL:unTWO:unRET:unADDRS}{PYNWmai0-ZQ3HACWSYBTTFFJTEM5GLS64PU000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{PULL{\_}TWO{\_}RET{\_}ADDRS}}{PULL:unTWO:unRET:unADDRS}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{290}\nwdocspar

\subsection{Dispatch table (\$06D3)}

The 18-byte table maps opcode indices to handler addresses in page {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}07\nwendquote}:

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{291}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-LZD7UO27WADGX7M4TS77RNCD74000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-LZD7UO27WADGX7M4TS77RNCD74000000-1}}}\moddef{resident dispatch table~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-LZD7UO27WADGX7M4TS77RNCD74000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $06D3
\nwlinkedidentc{RESIDENT_DISPATCH_TABLE}{PYNWmai0-LZD7UO27WADGX7M4TS77RNCD74000000-1}:
    HEX     00 27 55 5F 6D 8A AD B9
    HEX     4F A2 CE 26 79 A2 0F B5
    HEX     50 48
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH{\_}TABLE}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH:unTABLE}{PYNWmai0-LZD7UO27WADGX7M4TS77RNCD74000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH{\_}TABLE}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH:unTABLE}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{292}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegindocs{293}\nwdocspar

\begin{center}
\begin{tabular}{ccl}
\toprule
\thead{Opcode} & \thead{Table byte} & \thead{Handler address} \\
\midrule
\$00 & \$00 & \$0700 (RESIDENT\_DECODE\_DISPATCH) \\
\$01 & \$27 & \$0727 \\
\$02 & \$55 & \$0755 \\
\$03 & \$5F & \$075F \\
\$04 & \$6D & \$076D \\
\$05 & \$8A & \$078A \\
\$06 & \$AD & \$07AD \\
\$07 & \$B9 & \$07B9 \\
\$08 & \$4F & \$074F \\
\$09 & \$A2 & \$07A2 \\
\$0A & \$CE & \$07CE \\
\$0B & \$26 & \$0726 \\
\$0C & \$79 & \$0779 \\
\$0D & \$A2 & \$07A2 \\
\$0E & \$0F & \$070F \\
\$0F & \$B5 & \$07B5 \\
\$10 & \$50 & \$0750 \\
\$11 & \$48 & \$0748 \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
\end{center}

Opcodes \$09 and \$0D share the same handler (\$07A2).

\subsection{decode\_encrypted\_addr (\$0710)}

Decodes a 2-byte encrypted address from the bytecode stream.
Uses the same XOR scheme as the EALDR VM.  The decoded address is
left in {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}54/{\$}55\nwendquote}.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{294}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-QPGMZCBHONP3ALTVEWGVE7O2I4000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-QPGMZCBHONP3ALTVEWGVE7O2I4000000-1}}}\moddef{decode encrypted addr~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-QPGMZCBHONP3ALTVEWGVE7O2I4000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0710
\nwlinkedidentc{DECODE_ENCRYPTED_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-QPGMZCBHONP3ALTVEWGVE7O2I4000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     ($52),Y                 ; read low byte
    EOR     #$03                    ; decrypt
    INY
    BNE     .no_carry1
    INC     $53
.no_carry1:
    STA     $54                     ; decoded low
    LDA     ($52),Y                 ; read high byte
    INY
    BNE     .no_carry2
    INC     $53
.no_carry2:
    EOR     #$D9                    ; decrypt
    STA     $55                     ; decoded high
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{DECODE{\_}ENCRYPTED{\_}ADDR}}{DECODE:unENCRYPTED:unADDR}{PYNWmai0-QPGMZCBHONP3ALTVEWGVE7O2I4000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{DECODE{\_}ENCRYPTED{\_}ADDR}}{DECODE:unENCRYPTED:unADDR}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{295}\nwdocspar

\subsection{resident\_decode\_dispatch (\$0700)}

Opcode \$00 handler---the resident interpreter's GOTO instruction.
Decodes an address and redirects execution there.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{296}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-BGQWA2JRONNKYOAYDUITG47DXM000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-BGQWA2JRONNKYOAYDUITG47DXM000000-1}}}\moddef{resident decode dispatch~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-BGQWA2JRONNKYOAYDUITG47DXM000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0700
\nwlinkedidentc{RESIDENT_DECODE_DISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-BGQWA2JRONNKYOAYDUITG47DXM000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DECODE_ENCRYPTED_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-QPGMZCBHONP3ALTVEWGVE7O2I4000000-1}   ; → $54/$55
    LDA     $54                     ; \\
    STA     $52                     ;  | $52/$53 = decoded address
    LDA     $55                     ;  |
    STA     $53                     ; /
    LDY     #$00
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{RESIDENT_DISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}.fetch ; fetch from new location
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DECODE{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDECODE:unDISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-BGQWA2JRONNKYOAYDUITG47DXM000000-1}\eatline

\section{Script/event engine (\$795B)}
\label{sec:script_engine}

The script engine runs short bytecode programs that control animations,
sound, and game events.  It is called with a script index in X.

\subsection{Entry and setup}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{298}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}}}\moddef{script engine~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{\relax}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-2}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $795B
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ENGINE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}:
    SUBROUTINE

    STA     $C010                   ; clear keyboard strobe
    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{ATTRACT_FLAG}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}            ; attract_flag = 0
    CPX     #$06                    ; script index 6 = attract
    BNE     .not_attract
    INC     \nwlinkedidentc{ATTRACT_FLAG}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}            ; attract_flag = 1
.not_attract:

    CPX     #$02                    ; special setup for index 2
    BEQ     .setup_2
    CPX     #$04                    ; special setup for index 4
    BEQ     .setup_4
    JMP     .load_ptr

.setup_2:
    DEY
    STY     $80D5
    JMP     .load_ptr
.setup_4:
    DEY
    STY     $80E3
\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}FLAG}}{ATTRACT:unFLAG}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}FLAG}}{ATTRACT:unFLAG}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{299}\nwdocspar

\subsection{Script pointer table}

The script base address is loaded from the table at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}80AE\nwendquote}:

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{300}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-2}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-2}}}\moddef{script engine~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-3}\nwenddeflinemarkup

.load_ptr:
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_TABLE}{PYNWmai0-33FGP2UXYD5EEQJUC5DEXEFVLE000000-1},X          ; low byte
    STA     $E4
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_TABLE}{PYNWmai0-33FGP2UXYD5EEQJUC5DEXEFVLE000000-1}+1,X        ; high byte
    STA     $E5                     ; $E4/$E5 = script start address
\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}TABLE}}{SCRIPT:unTABLE}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}TABLE}}{SCRIPT:unTABLE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-2}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{301}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{302}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-33FGP2UXYD5EEQJUC5DEXEFVLE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-33FGP2UXYD5EEQJUC5DEXEFVLE000000-1}}}\moddef{script pointer table~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-33FGP2UXYD5EEQJUC5DEXEFVLE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $80AE
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_TABLE}{PYNWmai0-33FGP2UXYD5EEQJUC5DEXEFVLE000000-1}:
    DC.W    $80C6                   ; script 0
    DC.W    $80C7                   ; script 1
    DC.W    $80D7                   ; script 2
    DC.W    $A300                   ; script 3 (attract -- EALDR resident)
