\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}TABLE}}{SCRIPT:unTABLE}{PYNWmai0-33FGP2UXYD5EEQJUC5DEXEFVLE000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}TABLE}}{SCRIPT:unTABLE}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{303}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegindocs{304}\nwdocspar

Scripts 3--7 are in the {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A300\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A5FF\nwendquote} resident region (which was
also copied to {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}0500\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}07FF\nwendquote} by EALDR, but the script table
points to the original addresses).

\subsection{Script interpreter}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{305}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-21}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-23}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_CTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}     EQU     $5A8D   ; script loop iteration counter
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}    EQU     $5A8E   ; script loop address (2 bytes)
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_GOSUB_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}   EQU     $5A90   ; script gosub return address (2 bytes)
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_PRNG_MASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}    EQU     $5A92   ; PRNG mask for action randomization
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ACTION_VEC}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}   EQU     $5A93   ; action handler vector (2 bytes)
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}VEC}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unVEC}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}GOSUB{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unGOSUB:unADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}CTR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unCTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}VEC}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unVEC}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}GOSUB{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unGOSUB:unADDR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unADDR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}CTR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unCTR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{306}\nwdocspar

After setup, the interpreter initializes its loop counter and PRNG mask:

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{307}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-3}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-3}}}\moddef{script engine~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-2}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-4}\nwenddeflinemarkup

    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_CTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}         ; loop counter = 0
    LDA     #$01
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_PRNG_MASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}        ; PRNG mask = 1
.fetch:
    LDY     #$00
    LDA     ($E4),Y                 ; read script byte
    CMP     #$27
    BCC     .control                ; < $27 → control command
    JMP     .action                 ; ≥ $27 → action dispatch
\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}CTR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unCTR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}CTR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unCTR}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-3}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-3}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{308}\nwdocspar

\subsubsection{Control commands (< \$27)}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{309}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-4}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-4}}}\moddef{script engine~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-3}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwenddeflinemarkup

.control:
    CMP     #$25
    BEQ     .cmd_25                 ; set PRNG mask = $0F
    BCS     .cmd_26                 ; $26: PRNG mask = $00

    CMP     #$23
    BEQ     .cmd_23                 ; set action vector → $7A7F
    BCS     .cmd_24                 ; set action vector → $7A91

    CMP     #$21
    BEQ     .cmd_21                 ; gosub
    BCS     .cmd_22                 ; nop (return)

    CMP     #$1F
    BEQ     .cmd_1F                 ; set loop address
    BCS     .cmd_20                 ; set gosub address

    ; --- Loop/end-loop (byte < $1F) ---
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_CTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}         ; compare with loop counter
    BEQ     .end_loop
    BCC     .end_loop

    INC     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_CTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}         ; counter++
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}        ; \\
    STA     $E4                     ;  | $E4/$E5 = loop address
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}+1      ;  |
    STA     $E5                     ; /
    JMP     .fetch

.end_loop:
    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_CTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}         ; reset loop counter
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}
\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ADVANCE}}{SCRIPT:unADVANCE}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unADDR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}CTR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unCTR}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ADVANCE}}{SCRIPT:unADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-4}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unADDR}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-4}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}CTR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unCTR}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-4}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{310}\nwdocspar

When the byte value equals or exceeds the loop counter, the loop
terminates and the counter resets.  Otherwise, the counter increments
and execution jumps back to the saved loop address.

\subsubsection{Command implementations}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{311}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}}}\moddef{script engine~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-4}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwenddeflinemarkup

.cmd_25:                            ; PRNG mask = $0F
    LDA     #$0F
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_PRNG_MASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}

.cmd_26:                            ; PRNG mask = $00
    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_PRNG_MASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}

.cmd_23:                            ; action vector → $7A7F
    \nwlinkedidentc{STOW}{PYNWmai0-UDRZI6QCMYPCHBPEW5VLDMJPJU000000-1}    $7A7F,\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ACTION_VEC}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}

.cmd_24:                            ; action vector → $7A91
    \nwlinkedidentc{STOW}{PYNWmai0-UDRZI6QCMYPCHBPEW5VLDMJPJU000000-1}    $7A91,\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ACTION_VEC}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}

.cmd_22:                            ; nop (return from script)
    RTS

.cmd_21:                            ; gosub: jump to saved address
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_GOSUB_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}
    STA     $E4
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_GOSUB_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}+1
    STA     $E5
    JMP     .fetch

.cmd_1F:                            ; set loop address = current+1
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_INC_E4}{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}
    LDA     $E4
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}
    LDA     $E5
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}+1
    JMP     .fetch

.cmd_20:                            ; set gosub address = current+1
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_INC_E4}{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}
    LDA     $E4
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_GOSUB_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}
    LDA     $E5
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_GOSUB_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}+1
    JMP     .fetch
\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}VEC}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unVEC}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ADVANCE}}{SCRIPT:unADVANCE}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}GOSUB{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unGOSUB:unADDR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}INC{\_}E4}}{SCRIPT:unINC:unE4}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unADDR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}}\\{{\nwixident{STOW}}{STOW}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}VEC}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unVEC}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ADVANCE}}{SCRIPT:unADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}GOSUB{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unGOSUB:unADDR}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}INC{\_}E4}}{SCRIPT:unINC:unE4}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unADDR}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{STOW}}{STOW}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{312}\nwdocspar

\subsubsection{Action dispatch ($\geq$ \$27)}

When the script byte is {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}27\nwendquote} or higher, the PRNG output is masked and
XORed with the action byte, introducing randomness.  The action vector
at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}F6\nwendquote} is set by the handlers at {\Tt{}SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}ACTION{\textbackslash}{\_}VEC\nwendquote}.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{313}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}}}\moddef{script engine~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}{\relax}\nwenddeflinemarkup

.action:
    STA     $E2                     ; save action byte
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{STEP_PRNG}{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_OUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}             ; PRNG output
    AND     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_PRNG_MASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}        ; apply mask
    EOR     $E2                     ; XOR with action byte
    STA     $E1                     ; modified action
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_INC_E4}{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}           ; advance script pointer
    LDY     #$00
    LDA     ($E4),Y                 ; read parameter byte
    STA     $E2
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ACTION_INDIRECT}{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}  ; → JMP (\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ACTION_VEC}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22})
    JMP     ($F6)                   ; dispatch via action vector
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}INDIRECT}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unINDIRECT}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}VEC}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unVEC}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}INC{\_}E4}}{SCRIPT:unINC:unE4}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}}\\{{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}INDIRECT}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unINDIRECT}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}VEC}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unVEC}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}INC{\_}E4}}{SCRIPT:unINC:unE4}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{314}\nwdocspar

\subsection{advance (\$7A4F)}

The ``advance'' routine is the target of all {\Tt{}JMP\ SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}ADVANCE\nwendquote} in
the control commands.  It increments the script pointer, checks for user
input (during attract mode), and loops back to {\Tt{}.fetch\nwendquote}.

During the attract screen ({\Tt{}ATTRACT{\textbackslash}{\_}FLAG\nwendquote} = 1), this routine checks for
keyboard or joystick input.  If detected, it returns immediately via RTS,
which exits the entire {\Tt{}SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}ENGINE\nwendquote} call.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{315}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}}}\moddef{script advance~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $7A4F
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_INC_E4}{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}           ; advance script pointer
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ATTRACT_FLAG}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}            ; attract_flag
    BEQ     .continue               ; not attract mode → skip input check

    ; Attract mode: check keyboard
    LDA     $C000                   ; keyboard register
    BPL     .check_joy              ; no key → check joystick
    RTS                             ; key pressed → exit

.check_joy:
    LDA     $5A00                   ; joystick flag
    BEQ     .continue               ; no joystick → continue script
    LDX     #$00
    LDA     $C061,X                 ; button 0
    BPL     .btn1                   ; not pressed
    RTS                             ; pressed → exit
.btn1:
    INX
    LDA     $C061,X                 ; button 1
    BPL     .continue               ; not pressed → continue
    RTS                             ; pressed → exit

.continue:
    LSR     $5A8C                   ; shift timing flag
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ENGINE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}.fetch     ; loop back to interpreter
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ADVANCE}}{SCRIPT:unADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ADVANCE}}{SCRIPT:unADVANCE}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}FLAG}}{ATTRACT:unFLAG}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}INC{\_}E4}}{SCRIPT:unINC:unE4}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}FLAG}}{ATTRACT:unFLAG}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}INC{\_}E4}}{SCRIPT:unINC:unE4}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{316}\nwdocspar

\section{Scene data loading (\$6DD8)}

Loads scene-specific data from disk into the {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}5C00\nwendquote} region.  The disk
read calls {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}B300\nwendquote}, which is part of the EALDR disk I/O code still
resident in memory.  If the read fails, the routine fills a byte with
PRNG output (a graceful degradation rather than crashing).

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{319}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}}}\moddef{load scene data~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $6DD8
\nwlinkedidentc{LOAD_SCENE_DATA}{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    BIT     $C0E9                   ; check disk controller
    LDA     #$05                    ; \\
    LDY     #$04                    ;  | ($08)+4 = 5 (track configuration)
    STA     ($08),Y                 ; /
    LDA     #$00
    JSR     $6C18                   ; prepare disk parameters
    CLC
    JSR     $B300                   ; EALDR disk read routine
    BCS     .error
    RTS

.error:
    LDY     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_OUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}             ; on error: fill with PRNG data
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{STEP_PRNG}{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_OUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}
    STA     $9AA6,Y
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{LOAD{\_}SCENE{\_}DATA}}{LOAD:unSCENE:unDATA}{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{LOAD{\_}SCENE{\_}DATA}}{LOAD:unSCENE:unDATA}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}}\\{{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{320}\nwdocspar

\section{Unresolved: \$A478}
\label{sec:a478}

The scene loop calls {\Tt{}JSR\ {\textbackslash}{\$}A478\nwendquote} every iteration to check for user
input.  This address is in the EALDR region ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A000\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BFFF\nwendquote}),
which remains in memory after the main program starts.

The bytes at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A478\nwendquote} include the undocumented NMOS 6502 opcode {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}04\nwendquote}
(a 2-byte NOP).  This could mean the code legitimately uses undocumented
instructions, or that the region is modified at runtime before being called.

Partial decode:

\begin{verbatim}
    A478: 04 E5         ; NOP $E5 (DOP: 2-byte NOP, reads zp $E5)
    A47A: 19 03 64      ; ORA $6403,Y
    ...
    A483: CA            ; DEX
    A484: D0 FD         ; BNE $A483   (inner delay loop)
    A486: 38            ; SEC
    A487: E9 01         ; SBC #$01
    A489: D0 F6         ; BNE $A481   (outer delay loop)
    A48B: 60            ; RTS
\end{verbatim}

The inner loop at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A483\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A484\nwendquote} ({\Tt{}DEX;\ BNE\nwendquote}) is a standard
delay loop.  The outer loop decrements A and repeats, making this a
nested delay.  The carry flag state on exit likely indicates whether a
key was pressed (C=1) or the timer expired (C=0).  Further analysis
requires an emulator that supports undocumented 6502 opcodes.

\section{Summary}

The attract screen call flow:

\begin{itemize}
  \item {\Tt{}MAIN{\textbackslash}{\_}ENTRY\nwendquote} ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}0800\nwendquote}): calls {\Tt{}GAME{\textbackslash}{\_}INIT\nwendquote}, then
        {\Tt{}ATTRACT{\textbackslash}{\_}SCREEN\nwendquote} if {\Tt{}TOTAL{\textbackslash}{\_}MOB{\textbackslash}{\_}COUNT\nwendquote} is zero.
  \item {\Tt{}ATTRACT{\textbackslash}{\_}SCREEN\nwendquote} ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}09F4\nwendquote}): sets scene index 1, calls
        {\Tt{}COMPUTE{\textbackslash}{\_}SCENE{\textbackslash}{\_}PTR\nwendquote}, tail-calls {\Tt{}SCENE{\textbackslash}{\_}LOOP\nwendquote} with scene \$26.
  \item {\Tt{}SCENE{\textbackslash}{\_}LOOP\nwendquote} ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}6C37\nwendquote}): saves ZP pointers, steps PRNG,
        conditionally loads scene data from disk.  In a loop: checks
        keyboard/timer via {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A478\nwendquote}, displays status bar, renders scene
        text via {\Tt{}TEXT{\textbackslash}{\_}RENDERER\nwendquote}, runs {\Tt{}SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}ENGINE\nwendquote} with script \#3.
        Exits when user presses a key or scene sequence ends.
\end{itemize}

Key subsystems:
\begin{itemize}
  \item \textbf{Text renderer} ({\Tt{}TEXT{\textbackslash}{\_}RENDERER\nwendquote}): Reads byte streams with
        position commands, pause/reset control codes, and character data
        for the HRCG font.
  \item \textbf{Script engine} ({\Tt{}SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}ENGINE\nwendquote}): Runs short bytecode
        programs from {\Tt{}SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}TABLE\nwendquote}.  Supports loops, gosub, action
        dispatch with PRNG randomization.
  \item \textbf{Resident interpreter} ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}0500\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}07FF\nwendquote}): A
        secondary VM copied from EALDR, using context-swapped zero-page
        state and XOR-encrypted addresses.
  \item \textbf{PRNG} ({\Tt{}STEP{\textbackslash}{\_}PRNG\nwendquote}): Linear congruential generator with
        formula $\texttt{val}_{n+1} = 69 \cdot \texttt{val}_n + \$53
        \pmod{256}$.
\end{itemize}


\chapter{Animating the splash screen}

The {\Tt{}start{\_}splash{\_}screen\nwendquote} routine first loads up the initial splash screen,
sets {\Tt{}indirect{\_}routine\nwendquote} to {\Tt{}note{\_}played\nwendquote}, and begins the sound routine by
calling {\Tt{}start{\_}sound\nwendquote}.

{\Tt{}note{\_}played\nwendquote} plots a mob, then sets {\Tt{}indirect{\_}routine\nwendquote} to {\Tt{}splash{\_}routine{\_}2\nwendquote}
and jumps to {\Tt{}next{\_}table{\_}entry\nwendquote}.

{\Tt{}splash{\_}routine{\_}2\nwendquote} calls a routine first with {\Tt{}{\$}5E1F\nwendquote} then with {\Tt{}{\$}5E3A\nwendquote},
then jumps to {\Tt{}splash{\_}screen{\_}step\nwendquote}.

{\Tt{}splash{\_}screen{\_}step\nwendquote} then sets {\Tt{}indirect{\_}routine\nwendquote} to {\Tt{}splash{\_}routine{\_}1\nwendquote}
then {\Tt{}splash{\_}routine{\_}0\nwendquote} and calls {\Tt{}set{\_}splash{\_}routine\nwendquote} within {\Tt{}note{\_}played\nwendquote}.
After that, {\Tt{}splash{\_}screen{\_}step\nwendquote} presumably moves mobs around.


When the user ends the splash screen, the {\Tt{}start{\_}splash{\_}screen\nwendquote} routine
replaces the indirect jump to {\Tt{}indirect{\_}routine\nwendquote} in {\Tt{}start{\_}sound\nwendquote} to an
absolute jump to {\Tt{}next{\_}table{\_}entry\nwendquote}, since there is no further need to
animate while playing sound.

\subsection{Location data}

The first two bytes (bytes 0 and 1) in a {\Tt{}LOCATION{\_}DATA\nwendquote} record form a pointer to the location's
name string. If they are {\Tt{}FFFF\nwendquote}, then that is the end of the records. Byte 3 and byte 4 are
serial positions, where serial position is 20 times row plus column. I'm guessing this is the
top left and bottom right extents of the room.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{323}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ERFGCV2MLBMWTJDOVNONPK6K3I000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ERFGCV2MLBMWTJDOVNONPK6K3I000000-1}}}\moddef{Location data~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ERFGCV2MLBMWTJDOVNONPK6K3I000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwenddeflinemarkup

\chapter{Combat}

\section{Manual}

According to the original manual:

Strike probability

Whenever any character tries to strike another character, the game will
compute his chance of success. Any character's base chance of striking
his victim is 3.125% times their dexterity. Thus, a player with a dexterity of
11 has a 34.375% chance of striking his victim. However, the base chance is
adjusted by several factors:

If the victim is:

particularly difficult to hit

(halflings and elves have this ability to dodge) . . .. .. . ... subtract 12.5%
particularly easy to hit. . . . . . ....... . .. . .. .. .. .. . .. . . . .. . add 12.5%
extremely easy to hit ....... . . ... . . .. . . .. .. .. . .. . . . .. ... . add 25%
down (unconscious, in hand to hand combat, or resting) .. . . add 18.75%
currently resting (this is in
addition to the adjustment for being down) . . . .. .. . . . . . .. . add 9.375 %
defending . .. .. ..... .. .. . ... . . . ... . ........ . ..... subtract 9.375%
attacking ..... . ... . ... . ..... . ... ... ..... .... . . ... . no adjustment
running . . .... . .. . ..... .. .... . ... . .. .. .. . ..... . .. subtract 3.125 %
on the same space with attacker, the stronger character is
is given an advantage .. . .. . add 1.5625% times attackers strength and
subtract 1.5625% times victim's strength

The chance of striking the victim is then adjusted, if necessary, so that it
is never less than 3.125% nor greater than 96.875%.

The probabilities are in increments of 1/32. In the code, 1/32 is represented by
a single count in 6 bits, so the maximum count is 31 (96.875%).

DATA[0,1] = name
DATA[4] = creature type:
  0x00: Human
  0x01: Elf
  0x02: Dwarf
  0x03: Halfling
  0x15: Human
  0x23: Human (Morgiana, Princess Buddir)
  0x3C: Owl
  0x3F: Statue, Sultan, Right guard, Left guard, small zombie, big zombie
  0x41: Dwarf
  0x43: Thief
  0x44: Bear
  0x45: Rat
  0x46: Wolf
  0x47: Dragon
  0x48: Greasy
  0x4A: Sword
  0x4B: Ram
  0x4C: Scorpion
  0x4D: Succubus
  0x4E: Tiger, Leo, Jackal
  0x4F: Crab
  0x50: Bull
  0x54: Zombie (Witless)
  0x58: Thief
  0x59: Brown Bear
  0x5E: Wanderer
  0x5F: Mechanical Sword
  0x61: Scorpion (Giant)
  0x65: Sonny Boy Minotaur
  0x93: Statue (Gemini I, Gemini II)
  0x93: Aladdin
  0x94: Elf
  0x9B: White Dragon
  0x9E: Bane of Thieves
  0xA6: Unicorn

DATA[5] = STR
DATA[6] = CON/HP 0-3F
DATA[7] = MEL-1
DATA[9] = HTH-1
DATA[B] =
  7: Extremely easy to hit
  6: Particularly difficult to hit
  5: ? Incredibly easy to hit?
  4: DEX-1
  3: DEX-1
  2: DEX-1
  1: DEX-1
  0: DEX-1

DATA[C] = SPD
DATA[F] =
  7:
  6:
  5:
  4:
  3:
  2: Unconscious/Down
  1: State
  0: State

State:
  0:
  1:
  2:
  3: Defending

\subsection{set\_blink\_target (\$16A3)}

Sets up the blink cursor from the current combatant.  On the mob's turn,
the mob's packed position (byte 3 of mob data) is split into column and row,
and its appearance (byte 4) is converted to a font character number.
On the player's turn, the player's column and row are taken directly from
{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}5A63\nwendquote}/{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}5A64\nwendquote}, and the font character is looked up via {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}0C7E\nwendquote}.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{327}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-23}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-23}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-22}{\relax}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{IS_PLAYER_TURN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-23}  EQU     $5A74   ; 0 = mob's turn, 1 = player's turn
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{IS{\_}PLAYER{\_}TURN}}{IS:unPLAYER:unTURN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-23}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{IS{\_}PLAYER{\_}TURN}}{IS:unPLAYER:unTURN}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{328}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{329}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}}}\moddef{set blink target~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $16A3
\nwlinkedidentc{SET_BLINK_TARGET}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{IS_PLAYER_TURN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-23}
    CMP     #$01
    BEQ     .player

    ; --- mob path: convert packed position to col/row ---
    LDY     #$03
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ; mob data[3] = packed position
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{POS_TO_COLROW}{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}           ; A=col, Y=row
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{BLINK_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-5}
    STY     \nwlinkedidentc{BLINK_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-5}
    LDY     #$04
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ; mob data[4] = appearance
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{APPEARANCE_TO_FONTCHAR}{PYNWmai0-ZV3SLJLMHDXQXGXKZHHC4ROVNQ000000-1}  ; appearance → font char number
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{BLINK_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-5}
    RTS

    ; --- player path: col/row already separate ---
.player:
    LDA     $5A63                   ; player font column
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{BLINK_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-5}
    LDA     $5A64                   ; player font row
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{BLINK_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-5}
    LDA     $F4                     ; \\
    STA     $BE                     ;  | copy pointer $F4 → $BE
    LDA     $F5                     ;  |
    STA     $BF                     ; /
    JSR     $0C7E                   ; look up player's font char
    LDA     FONT_CHARNUM
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{BLINK_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-5}
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SET{\_}BLINK{\_}TARGET}}{SET:unBLINK:unTARGET}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SET{\_}BLINK{\_}TARGET}}{SET:unBLINK:unTARGET}}}\nwnotused{set blink target}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{APPEARANCE{\_}TO{\_}FONTCHAR}}{APPEARANCE:unTO:unFONTCHAR}}\\{{\nwixident{BLINK{\_}CHAR}}{BLINK:unCHAR}}\\{{\nwixident{BLINK{\_}COL}}{BLINK:unCOL}}\\{{\nwixident{BLINK{\_}ROW}}{BLINK:unROW}}\\{{\nwixident{IS{\_}PLAYER{\_}TURN}}{IS:unPLAYER:unTURN}}\\{{\nwixident{POS{\_}TO{\_}COLROW}}{POS:unTO:unCOLROW}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{APPEARANCE{\_}TO{\_}FONTCHAR}}{APPEARANCE:unTO:unFONTCHAR}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{BLINK{\_}CHAR}}{BLINK:unCHAR}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{BLINK{\_}COL}}{BLINK:unCOL}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{BLINK{\_}ROW}}{BLINK:unROW}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{IS{\_}PLAYER{\_}TURN}}{IS:unPLAYER:unTURN}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{POS{\_}TO{\_}COLROW}}{POS:unTO:unCOLROW}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{330}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{331}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-X4FLZFQK2PJN7VH3YTA5N5PTO4000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-X4FLZFQK2PJN7VH3YTA5N5PTO4000000-1}}}\moddef{Hit chance~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-X4FLZFQK2PJN7VH3YTA5N5PTO4000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwenddeflinemarkup
(15AB)
.compute_to_hit:
    JSR      \nwlinkedidentc{SET_BLINK_TARGET}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}
    LDA      \nwlinkedidentc{IS_PLAYER_TURN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-23}
    CMP      #$01
    BNE      .mob
    LDA      #$1C
    STA      TO_HIT
    JMP      .roll

.mob:
    ; Base chance = dexterity (-1)
    LDY      #$0B
    LDA      (MOB_PTR?),Y
    TAX
    AND      #$1F
    STA      TO_HIT
    TXA

    ; If DEX bit 5 set, clear DEX bit 4
    ; and add 75% to chance.
    AND      #$20
    BEQ      LAB_15d6
    TXA
    AND      #$EF
    STA      (MOB_PTR?),Y
    LDA      #$18
    JSR      add_to_to_hit

LAB_15d6:
    ; If opponent DEX bit 6 set,
    ; subtract 12.5% (particularly difficult
    ; to hit).
    LDA      (THING_PTR?),Y
    TAY
    AND      #$40
    BEQ      LAB_15e2
    LDA      #$FC
    JSR      add_to_to_hit

LAB_15e2:
    ; If opponent DEX bit 7 set,
    ; add 25% (extremely easy to hit).
    TYA
    AND      #$80
    BEQ      .check_thing_f
    LDA      #$08
    JSR      add_to_to_hit

.check_thing_f:
    ; If opponent F bit 2 set,
    ; add 18.75% (down: unconscious, in hand to hand combat,
    ; or resting)
    LDY      #$0F
    LDA      (THING_PTR?),Y
    TAX
    AND      #$04
    BEQ      LAB_15fa
    LDA      #$06
    JSR      add_to_to_hit

LAB_15fa:
    ; If opponent F bits 1,0 < 1
    ; add 9.375% (currently resting)
    TXA
    AND      #$03
    CMP      #$01
    BPL      LAB_1609
    LDA      #$03
    JSR      add_to_to_hit
    JMP      .check_thing_6

LAB_1609:
    ; subtract 3.125% ("running" -- bugged?)
    BNE      LAB_1613
    LDA      #$FF
    JSR      add_to_to_hit
    JMP      .check_thing_6

LAB_1613:
    ; If opponent F bits 1,0 == 3
    ; subtract 9.375% (opponent is defending)
    CMP      #$03
    BNE      .check_thing_6
    LDA      #$FD
    JSR      add_to_to_hit

.check_thing_6:
    ; If opponent CON <= 3
    ; add 75%.
    LDY      #$06
    LDA      (THING_PTR?),Y
    AND      #$3F
    CMP      #$03
    BCS      LAB_162b
    LDA      #$18
    JSR      add_to_to_hit

LAB_162b:
    ; If mob[3] == thing[3]...
    LDY      #$03
    LDA      (MOB_PTR?),Y
    CMP      (THING_PTR?),Y
    BNE      .limit_to_hit

    ; add Thing[STR]/2 & 0x0F - Mob[STR]/2 & 0x0F
    LDY      #$05
    LDA      (THING_PTR?),Y
    ROR      A
    AND      #$0F
    STA      DAT_5a77
    LDA      (MOB_PTR?),Y
    ROR      A
    AND      #$0F
    SEC
    SBC      DAT_5a77
    JSR      add_to_to_hit

.limit_to_hit:
    LDA      TO_HIT
    BPL      .adjust_for_automatic_fail
    LDA      #$00
    STA      TO_HIT
    JMP      .roll

.adjust_for_automatic_fail:
    CMP      #$1F
    BMI      .roll
    LDA      #$1E
    STA      TO_HIT

.roll:
    LDA      #$1F
    JSR      get_random
    CMP      TO_HIT
    BMI      .do_hit
    BEQ      .do_hit
    JSR      clear_row_21
    JSR      print_name_of_actor
    JSR      scroll_status_window_up
    LDA      #$D2
    STA      DATA_PTR2
    LDA      #$7C
    STA      DATA_PTR2+1
    JSR      print_centered_row_23
    JSR      scroll_status_window_up
    LDA      #$01
    CMP      \nwlinkedidentc{IS_PLAYER_TURN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-23}
    BEQ      .do_blink
    JSR      print_thing_name_centered_row_23
.do_blink:
    JSR      blink
    RTS
.do_hit:
    LDA      \nwlinkedidentc{IS_PLAYER_TURN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-23}
    BEQ      .hit_mob
    JMP      hit_nonmob?
.hit_mob:
    JMP      hit_mob?
\nwnotused{Hit chance}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{IS{\_}PLAYER{\_}TURN}}{IS:unPLAYER:unTURN}}\\{{\nwixident{SET{\_}BLINK{\_}TARGET}}{SET:unBLINK:unTARGET}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{IS{\_}PLAYER{\_}TURN}}{IS:unPLAYER:unTURN}{PYNWmai0-X4FLZFQK2PJN7VH3YTA5N5PTO4000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SET{\_}BLINK{\_}TARGET}}{SET:unBLINK:unTARGET}{PYNWmai0-X4FLZFQK2PJN7VH3YTA5N5PTO4000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{332}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{333}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-QT6ETJXFJSZ45KITEMECPS3GYA000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-QT6ETJXFJSZ45KITEMECPS3GYA000000-1}}}\moddef{Get item at pos in room~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-QT6ETJXFJSZ45KITEMECPS3GYA000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG      $0B62
    ; Takes A (pos) and \nwlinkedidentc{TMP_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2} (pointer to room data)
get_item_at_pos_in_room:
    SUBROUTINE

    STA      \nwlinkedidentc{DAT_5a17_pos}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}

    ; load1 <- \nwlinkedidentc{TMP_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}
    ; load3 <- \nwlinkedidentc{TMP_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}

    LDA      \nwlinkedidentc{TMP_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}+1
    STA      .load1+2
    STA      .load3+2
    LDA      \nwlinkedidentc{TMP_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}
    STA      .load1+1
    STA      .load3+1
    JMP      .get_mob_link

.inner_loop:
    ; load2 <- room data[MAP]

    LDX      #$06
.load1:
    LDA      .load1+1,X
    STA      .load2+1-6,X
    INX
    BNE.X    #$08, .load1

.load2:
    ; Y <- (load2)

    LDY      .load2+1
    BNE.Y    #$FF, .not_ff          ; (load2) != 0xFF?
    JMP      \nwlinkedidentc{is_at_outer_limits}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}     ; else goto \nwlinkedidentc{is_at_outer_limits}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}

.not_ff:
    BEQ.Y    \nwlinkedidentc{DAT_5a17_pos}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}, .return_load2  ; (load2) == \nwlinkedidentc{DAT_5a17_pos}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}?

    ; load2 += 3

    \nwlinkedidentc{INCW}{PYNWmai0-UDRZI6QCMYPCHBPEW5VLDMJPJU000000-8}     .load2
    \nwlinkedidentc{INCW}{PYNWmai0-UDRZI6QCMYPCHBPEW5VLDMJPJU000000-8}     .load2
    INC      .load2+1
    BNE      .load2
    INC      .load2+2
    JMP      .load2

.return_load2:
    ; \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2} <- load2

    \nwlinkedidentc{STOW}{PYNWmai0-UDRZI6QCMYPCHBPEW5VLDMJPJU000000-1}     .load2+1, \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}
    RTS

.get_mob_link:

    LDX      #$02
.load3:
    LDA      .load3+1,X  ; A <- load3[MOB]
    BEQ.A    #$00, .inner_loop
    JSR      mob_dataptr_to_load4

    LDX      #$03
.load4:
    LDY      .load4+1,X  ; Y <- load4[POS]
    BEQ.Y    \nwlinkedidentc{DAT_5a17_pos}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-8}, .return_load4

    ; load3 <- load4

    \nwlinkedidentc{STOW}{PYNWmai0-UDRZI6QCMYPCHBPEW5VLDMJPJU000000-1}     .load4+1, .load3+1
    JMP      .get_mob_link

.return_load4:
    ; \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2} = 0x8000 | load4

    LDA      #$80
    ORA      .load4+2
    STA      \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}+1
    LDA      .load4+1
    STA      \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}
    RTS

mob_dataptr_to_load4:
    SUBROUTINE
    ; load4 <- mob data for A

    JSR      \nwlinkedidentc{GET_MOB_DATA}{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}
    \nwlinkedidentc{STOW}{PYNWmai0-UDRZI6QCMYPCHBPEW5VLDMJPJU000000-1}     \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR3}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}, .load4
    RTS

\subsection{get\_mob\_data (\$0C32)}

Converts a 1-based mob index in {\Tt{}A\nwendquote} to a pointer to its 16-byte data
record, stored in {\Tt{}DATA{\textbackslash}{\_}PTR3\nwendquote} ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BA/{\textbackslash}{\$}BB\nwendquote}).  The mob data table
starts at the address stored in {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}4000/{\textbackslash}{\$}4001\nwendquote} (within the decrypted
game data region), with each record being 16 bytes.  The formula is:

\begin{center}
{\Tt{}DATA{\textbackslash}{\_}PTR3\nwendquote} = {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}4000/{\textbackslash}{\$}4001\nwendquote} + (A $-$ 1) $\times$ 16
\end{center}

The multiplication by 16 is done by rotating the decremented index
left by 4 bits through carry, then splitting the result into high and
low byte contributions.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{335}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}}}\moddef{get mob data~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0C32
\nwlinkedidentc{GET_MOB_DATA}{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    CLC
    ADC     #$FF                    ; A = index - 1, C = 1
    ROL                             ; \\
    ROL                             ;  | rotate \{C, A\} left 4 bits
    ROL                             ;  | = (index-1) * 16 with bits split
    ROL                             ; /
    TAY                             ; save rotated value
    ROL                             ; one more rotate
    AND     #$0F                    ; high byte contribution = (index-1) >> 4
    CLC
    ADC     $4001                   ; add base page
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR3}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}+1
    TYA
    AND     #$F0                    ; low byte contribution = ((index-1) & $0F) << 4
    CLC
    ADC     $4000                   ; add base offset
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR3}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}
    BCC     .done
    INC     \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR3}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}+1             ; carry to high byte
.done:
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{GET{\_}MOB{\_}DATA}}{GET:unMOB:unDATA}{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{GET{\_}MOB{\_}DATA}}{GET:unMOB:unDATA}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{DATA{\_}PTR3}}{DATA:unPTR3}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{DATA{\_}PTR3}}{DATA:unPTR3}{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{336}\nwdocspar

\subsection{init\_mob\_count (\$0C51)}

Called once during {\Tt{}GAME{\textbackslash}{\_}INIT\nwendquote} to initialize {\Tt{}TOTAL{\textbackslash}{\_}MOB{\textbackslash}{\_}COUNT\nwendquote}.
Walks all 9-byte character records starting from index~1 (skipping
the group-0 header at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}4000\nwendquote}), summing byte~8 (group member count)
of each record until the end sentinel (byte~1 = {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}FF\nwendquote}) is reached.

The result is the total number of mobs assigned to groups~1 and above.
At startup, byte~8 contains only the group count in bits~3--0 (the
upper bits---pending XP and status flag---are zero), so the sum is
simply the total mob count.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{337}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-FUVGEE5QFLBSHT5MZWRVT5CDCY000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-FUVGEE5QFLBSHT5MZWRVT5CDCY000000-1}}}\moddef{init mob count~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-FUVGEE5QFLBSHT5MZWRVT5CDCY000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0C51
\nwlinkedidentc{INIT_MOB_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-FUVGEE5QFLBSHT5MZWRVT5CDCY000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     #$00                    ; \\
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{TOTAL_MOB_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}         ; / clear total
    LDA     #$09                    ; \\ $FA/$FB = $4009 (record 1)
    STA     $FA                     ;  |
    LDA     #$40                    ;  |
    STA     $FB                     ; /
.loop:
    LDY     #$01
    LDA     ($FA),Y                 ; byte 1 of record
    CMP     #$FF                    ; $FF = end sentinel
    BNE     .count
    RTS
.count:
    LDY     #$08
    LDA     ($FA),Y                 ; byte 8 = group member count
    CLC
    ADC     \nwlinkedidentc{TOTAL_MOB_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}         ; accumulate
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{TOTAL_MOB_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}
    LDA     #$09                    ; \\ advance $FA by 9 (next record)
    ADC     $FA                     ;  |
    STA     $FA                     ;  |
    BCC     .loop                   ;  |
    INC     $FB                     ;  |
    BCS     .loop                   ; / always taken
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{INIT{\_}MOB{\_}COUNT}}{INIT:unMOB:unCOUNT}{PYNWmai0-FUVGEE5QFLBSHT5MZWRVT5CDCY000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{INIT{\_}MOB{\_}COUNT}}{INIT:unMOB:unCOUNT}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{TOTAL{\_}MOB{\_}COUNT}}{TOTAL:unMOB:unCOUNT}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TOTAL{\_}MOB{\_}COUNT}}{TOTAL:unMOB:unCOUNT}{PYNWmai0-FUVGEE5QFLBSHT5MZWRVT5CDCY000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{338}\nwdocspar
